校订说明
本稿以所定英汉双语底本为校勘主线，处理《周易》六十四卦的卦辞、爻辞，未收入《彖传》 《象
传》 《文言》 《系辞》等十翼全文。终校时按卦序、卦名、卦画、卦辞、爻位、爻辞、用九用六逐项
核对，并同时检查英文直译、自然意译与深度文化译文之间的术语一致性、语义对应关系与跨文
化可读性。
本稿采用现代简体中文排印。底本或通行本中作为古字、异体或传统字形出现者，若有明确简化
字而不损害经义，径用简化字；传统异体字形已统一为“遁” “颠” 。若属于《易》经文专字、古
义字或无稳定现代简化替代者，则保留其经文形态，如“无” “輹” “鬯” “虩” “眚” “𫗧”等。此
处所谓“不用繁体字” ，指正文说明、术语解释与可简化经文字形均不用繁体排印；不是以现代白
话替换经文。
终校重点包括：逐字核查六十四卦卦辞、爻辞的字形、标点与爻位；统一“元、亨、利、贞、吉、
凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎、有孚、君子、大人、涉大川”等术语；检查英文译文是否既不脱离字面，
又不把《易》化约为占卜迷信、心理鸡汤或西方式宿命论；并保持每卦“关键词释义”逐项单独
成行，便于出版排版、索引、引用与人工复校。
关键词释义
信 忠实经文字面、象数语汇与义理结构；不擅自现代化、心理化或神秘化。
达 英语读者可自然理解处境智慧、德性修养与行动判断。
雅 英文力求庄重、凝练、典雅；中文说明力求审慎、清晰、可校。
底本范围 本稿处理六十四卦卦辞、爻辞；若作正式出版，仍宜另设经文校勘、异文说
明与十翼注释卷。
目录跳转 全书章标题、前后附录均进入 PDF 目录与书签，可点击跳转。
v

凡例与译法总则
每卦依次列出：原文、关键词释义、贴近原文的英文直译、面向英语母语者的自然意译、最终推荐
的深度文化译文、英文哲学与文化注解、中文翻译取舍说明。术语如君子、大人、无咎、悔、吝、
利贞、涉大川等，原则上保持稳定译法，以便读者追踪六十四卦内部的概念网络。
关键词释义
元 创始、根本、广大；英译以 originary/primal 为主。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译以 through-going 为主。
利 合宜而有益；英译以 favorable/furthering 为主，不作 profit。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译以 constancy 为主。
吉 趋向善成的处境判断；英译为 good fortune，避免 luck 的偶然色彩。
凶 趋向败坏或危险的处境判断；英译为misfortune，避免fatal doom或 fa-
talistic doom。
无咎 虽处险境而行为得宜， 故无可归咎；英译为no blame/no blame attaches。
君子 修德成位者；英译为 the noble one。
大人 德位相称、足以定向共同体者；英译为 the Great Person。
时位 行动之得失取决于时、位、德、应；同一象在不同爻位可有不同判断。
vi

第1 卦
䷀ 乾 (Qian)
The Creative Heaven
原文
乾，元亨利贞。
初九，潜龙勿用。
九二，见龙在田，利见大人。
九三，君子终日乾乾，夕惕若，厉，无咎。
九四，或跃在渊，无咎。
九五，飞龙在天，利见大人。
上九，亢龙有悔。
用九，见群龙无首，吉。
关键词释义
卦名 乾（Qian） ：刚健创始之德；以天道不息象示创生、时位、节制与自强。
英译标题 The Creative Heaven。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保
留专名身份。
乾 健也；象天之刚健不息，非单纯自然天空。
龙 乾德之象；能潜、能见、能跃、能飞，重在时位变化。
用九 全卦阳爻之用，重在刚健能化而不自居其首。
无首 非无序，而是不以一己居首、刚而能和。
元亨利贞 四德并举：创始、通达、合宜、正固，构成《易》之基本价值序列。
元亨 元而能通，表示大端已具而其道可行。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
1

2 第1 卦
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
利见大人 宜亲近、咨取或得见德位相称者，以定方向。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
大人 德位相称、能定大局者；英译作 the Great Person。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Qian: originary, through-going, favorable, and steadfast.
Initial Nine: a hidden dragon; do not put it to use.
Second Nine: the dragon appears in the field; it is favorable to see the Great Person.
Third Nine: the noble one is vigorous all day and alert at night; peril, yet no blame
attaches.
Fourth Nine: perhaps leaping in the abyss; no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: the dragon flies in heaven; it is favorable to see the Great Person.
Top Nine: the overreaching dragon has regret.
Use of the Nines: a host of dragons is seen, none taking the head; good fortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, The Creative Heaven may be read as a pattern of action rather
than a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral mea-
sure govern success or danger.
Qian: originary, through-going, favorable, and steadfast.
Initial Nine: a hidden dragon; do not put it to use.

3
Second Nine: the dragon appears in the field; it is favorable to see the Great Person.
Third Nine: the noble one is vigorous all day and alert at night; peril, yet no blame
attaches.
Fourth Nine: perhaps leaping in the abyss; no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: the dragon flies in heaven; it is favorable to see the Great Person.
Top Nine: the overreaching dragon has regret.
Use of the Nines: a host of dragons is seen, none taking the head; good fortune.
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Qian: originary, through-going, favorable, and steadfast.
Initial Nine: a hidden dragon; do not put it to use.
Second Nine: the dragon appears in the field; it is favorable to see the Great Person.
Third Nine: the noble one is vigorous all day and alert at night; peril, yet no blame
attaches.
Fourth Nine: perhaps leaping in the abyss; no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: the dragon flies in heaven; it is favorable to see the Great Person.
Top Nine: the overreaching dragon has regret.
Use of the Nines: a host of dragons is seen, none taking the head; good fortune.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Qian is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, The Cre-
ative Heaven, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the
original term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble
one, the Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so
that an English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes
across all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical
divination or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image,
timing, position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、卦名、卦辞、爻位与爻辞逐项校入；本终校本采用简体
排印，标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。卦名保留拼音Qian，英文标题“The
Creative Heaven”只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“龙”按乾德之象处理，不按西方 dragon 的怪兽传统解释； “用九”重在刚健
能化、群龙不争首。

4 第1 卦
术语取舍。“元亨利贞”不拆成四个互不相干的吉祥词，而按创始、通达、合宜、正固的义
理序列处理。 “元亨”译作primal/originary and through-going，保留“大端可通”之
义。 “利贞”译为favorable through constancy，不译成profitable divination。 “无咎”
统一为no blame attaches， 不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “利见大人”译作favorable to
see/behold the Great Person，既保留见贤取法，也保留政治伦理中的定向作用。 “悔”译
为regret， 取可反省、 可转圜之悔， 不作最终灾祸。 “厉”译为peril， 不等同于misfortune；
它提示戒惧而非判定终局。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随
机好运。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第2 卦
䷁ 坤 (Kun)
The Receptive Earth
原文
坤，元亨，利牝马之贞。君子有攸往，先迷后得主利。西南得朋，东北丧朋，安贞吉。
初六，履霜，坚冰至。
六二，直方大，不习，无不利。
六三，含章可贞，或从王事，无成有终。
六四，括囊，无咎无誉。
六五，黄裳，元吉。
上六，龙战于野，其血玄黄。
用六，利永贞。
关键词释义
卦名 坤（Kun） ：柔顺承载之德；以地道厚载象示顺承、安贞与含弘。
英译标题 The Receptive Earth。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保
留专名身份。
坤 顺也；象地之承载、含弘与成物。
牝马 柔顺而能行远之象，顺承中有持久之健。
西南得朋 同类相从之方；偏重归附与聚合。
东北丧朋 离朋而得主之方；偏重去私从公。
黄裳 中正谦下之象，黄为中，裳为下。
元亨 元而能通，表示大端已具而其道可行。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
5

6 第2 卦
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Kun: originary and through-going; favorable is the constancy of a mare. If the no-
ble one has somewhere to go, he first loses the way and later gains a lord. In the
southwest he gains companions; in the northeast he loses companions. Peaceful
constancy is good fortune.
Initial Six: treading on frost; hard ice is coming.
Second Six: straight, square, and great; without rehearsal, nothing is unfavorable.
Third Six: holding brilliance within, one may be steadfast. If following the king’s
affairs, there is no claim of achievement, yet there is completion.
Fourth Six: a tied-up sack; no blame, no praise.
Fifth Six: a yellow lower garment; greatly good fortune.
Top Six: dragons battle in the field; their blood is dark and yellow.
Use of the Sixes: favorable is enduring constancy.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, The Receptive Earth may be read as a pattern of action rather
than a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral mea-
sure govern success or danger.

7

Third Six: holding brilliance within, one may be steadfast. If following the king’s

最终推荐的深度文化译文
Kun: primal and through-going; favorable is the constancy of a mare. If the no-
ble one has somewhere to go, he first loses the way and later gains a lord. In the
southwest he gains companions; in the northeast he loses companions. Peaceful
constancy is good fortune.
Initial Six: treading on frost; hard ice is coming.
Second Six: straight, square, and great; without rehearsal, nothing is unfavorable.
Third Six: holding brilliance within, one may be steadfast. If following the king’s
affairs, there is no claim of achievement, yet there is completion.
Fourth Six: a tied-up sack; no blame attaches, no praise.
Fifth Six: a yellow lower garment; greatly good fortune.
Top Six: dragons battle in the field; their blood is dark and yellow.
Use of the Sixes: favorable is enduring constancy.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Kun is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, The Re-
ceptive Earth, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the
original term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble
one, the Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so
that an English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes
across all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical
divination or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image,
timing, position, and conduct.

8 第2 卦
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、卦名、卦辞、爻位与爻辞逐项校入；本终校本采用简体
排印，标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。卦名保留拼音 Kun，英文标题“The
Receptive Earth”只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“牝马之贞”译出柔顺而健行的持续力，避免把坤解释成被动服从； “西南/东北”
保留方位象，不硬译成现代地理。
术语取舍。“元亨” 译作primal/originary and through-going， 保留 “大端可通” 之义。 “贞
吉”译作constancy brings good fortune，强调吉由守正而来。 “无咎”统一为no blame
attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “往”译为go / set out，说明其可否取决于时位，
不等于一般行动自由。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随机好
运。 “君子”译为the noble one，指修德成位者，避免 gentleman 的阶级和社交色彩。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第3 卦
䷂ 屯 (Zhun)
Difficulty at the Beginning
原文
屯，元亨，利贞。勿用有攸往，利建侯。
初九，磐桓，利居贞，利建侯。
六二，屯如邅如，乘马班如。匪寇婚媾，女子贞不字，十年乃字。
六三，即鹿无虞，惟入于林中。君子几不如舍，往吝。
六四，乘马班如，求婚媾。往吉，无不利。
九五，屯其膏，小贞吉，大贞凶。
上六，乘马班如，泣血涟如。
关键词释义
卦名 屯（Zhun） ：草木初生而艰难；象征创始阶段的阻力、聚合与秩序建立。
英译标题 Difficulty at the Beginning。 标题取意译， 以便英语读者先得卦象主旨； 拼
音保留专名身份。
屯 初生之难；不是失败，而是创始未定。
磐桓 徘徊不进，示慎重立基。
婚媾 结合、联盟之象，不宜只作男女情节。
建侯 建立秩序与代理治理。
元亨 元而能通，表示大端已具而其道可行。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
贞凶 虽持守而所守失时或失位，故成凶。
9

10 第3 卦
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
侯 侯伯之位；多指新秩序建立时的分封、任命与组织化。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Zhun: originary and through-going; favorable to maintain constancy. Do not hasten
to go somewhere; it is favorable to establish a lord.
Initial Nine: hesitating and circling; favorable to dwell in constancy; favorable to
establish a lord.
Second Six: difficulty and delay; horses draw back in ranks. It is not a robber but a
suitor. The woman is steadfast and does not conceive; after ten years she conceives.
Third Six: pursuing deer without a forester, one merely enters the forest. The noble
one sees the signs and would rather let go; to go on brings regret.
Fourth Six: horses draw back; seeking marriage alliance. To go is good fortune;
nothing is unfavorable.
Fifth Nine: hoarding the rich fat; small constancy is good fortune, great constancy
is misfortune.
Top Six: horses draw back; tears of blood flow.

11
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Difficulty at the Beginning may be read as a pattern of action
rather than a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral
measure govern success or danger.
Zhun: primal and through-going; favorable to maintain constancy. Do not hasten
to go somewhere; it is favorable to establish a lord.
Initial Nine: hesitating and circling; favorable to dwell in constancy; favorable to
establish a lord.
Second Six: difficulty and delay; horses draw back in ranks. It is not a robber but a
suitor. The woman is steadfast and does not conceive; after ten years she conceives.
Third Six: pursuing deer without a forester, one merely enters the forest. The noble
one sees the signs and would rather let go; to go on brings regret.
Fourth Six: horses draw back; seeking marriage alliance. To go is good fortune;
nothing is unfavorable.
Fifth Nine: hoarding the rich fat; small constancy is good fortune, great constancy
is misfortune.
Top Six: horses draw back; tears of blood flow.
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Zhun: primal and through-going; favorable to maintain constancy. Do not hasten
to go somewhere; it is favorable to establish a lord.
Initial Nine: hesitating and circling; favorable to dwell in constancy; favorable to
establish a lord.
Second Six: difficulty and delay; horses draw back in ranks. It is not a robber but a
suitor. The woman is steadfast and does not conceive; after ten years she conceives.
Third Six: pursuing deer without a forester, one merely enters the forest. The noble
one sees the signs and would rather let go; to go on brings regret.
Fourth Six: horses draw back; seeking marriage alliance. To go is good fortune;
nothing is unfavorable.
Fifth Nine: hoarding the rich fat; small constancy is good fortune, great constancy
is misfortune.
Top Six: horses draw back; tears of blood flow.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Zhun is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Difficulty
at the Beginning, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for
the original term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble

12 第3 卦
one, the Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so
that an English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes
across all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical
divination or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image,
timing, position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排
印， 标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。 卦名保留拼音Zhun， 英文标题 “Difficulty
at the Beginning”只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“屯”取草木初生而难出之象，译文以beginning difficulty处理，不译成单纯
灾难。
术语取舍。“元亨” 译作primal/originary and through-going， 保留 “大端可通” 之义。 “利
贞”译为 favorable through constancy，不译成 profitable divination。 “贞吉”译作
constancy brings good fortune，强调吉由守正而来。 “往”译为go / set out，说明其可
否取决于时位，不等于一般行动自由。 “吝”译为regret / shame / distress according to
context，重在窘迫与可羞之迹。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等
于随机好运。 “凶”译为misfortune，指行为与时位相违所趋向的败坏或危险。 “君子”译
为 the noble one，指修德成位者，避免 gentleman 的阶级和社交色彩。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第4 卦
䷃ 蒙 (Meng)
Youthful Envelopment
原文
蒙，亨。匪我求童蒙，童蒙求我。初筮告，再三渎，渎则不告，利贞。
初六，发蒙。利用刑人，用说桎梏，以往吝。
九二，包蒙，吉。纳妇吉，子克家。
六三，勿用取女，见金夫，不有躬，无攸利。
六四，困蒙，吝。
六五，童蒙，吉。
上九，击蒙，不利为寇，利御寇。
关键词释义
卦名 蒙（Meng） ：蒙昧未开；重在求教、启蒙、节制教育与受教之诚。
英译标题 Youthful Envelopment。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音
保留专名身份。
蒙 蒙昧未启；教育关系须以求教之诚为先。
初筮告 初问则告，重在诚与敬。
再三渎 反复亵问则不告，示学问不可玩弄。
发蒙 开启蒙昧，亦含必要的规训。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
13

14 第4 卦
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Meng: through-going. It is not I who seek the youthful ignorant; the youthful igno-
rant seek me. At the first divination I instruct; repeated importunity is profanation,
and when profaned I do not instruct. Favorable to be steadfast.
Initial Six: opening ignorance. It is useful to apply discipline and to remove fetters;
to continue in this way brings regret.
Second Nine: embracing the ignorant; good fortune. Taking a wife is good fortune;
the son can sustain the household.
Third Six: do not take this woman; seeing a man of gold, she does not possess her-
self. Nothing is favorable.
Fourth Six: trapped in ignorance; regret.
Fifth Six: childlike ignorance; good fortune.
Top Nine: striking ignorance. It is not favorable to be a robber; it is favorable to
defend against robbers.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Youthful Envelopment may be read as a pattern of action rather
than a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral mea-
sure govern success or danger.

rant seek me. At the first divination I instruct; repeated importunity is profanation,

to continue in this way brings regret.
Second Nine: embracing the ignorant; good fortune. Taking a wife is good fortune;
the son can sustain the household.
Third Six: do not take this woman; seeing a man of gold, she does not possess herself.
Nothing is favorable.

Fifth Six: childlike ignorance; good fortune.
Top Nine: striking ignorance. It is not favorable to be a robber; it is favorable to
defend against robbers.

第5 卦
䷄ 需 (Xu)
Waiting
原文
需，有孚，光亨，贞吉，利涉大川。
初九，需于郊，利用恒，无咎。
九二，需于沙，小有言，终吉。
九三，需于泥，致寇至。
六四，需于血，出自穴。
九五，需于酒食，贞吉。
上六，入于穴，有不速之客三人来。敬之，终吉。
关键词释义
卦名 需（Xu） ：有所待；非消极等待，而是以孚信养时、守中待机。
英译标题 Waiting。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
需 等待；在险前养诚，不是消极拖延。
酒食 等待中有养与安，不轻躁犯险。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
涉大川 涉险成事；指重大行动与跨越艰难处境。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
17

18 第5 卦
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Xu: there is trust; luminous success. Constancy is good fortune; favorable to cross
the great river.
Initial Nine: waiting in the outskirts; favorable to use constancy; no blame attaches.
Second Nine: waiting on the sand; some small words, yet finally good fortune.
Third Nine: waiting in the mud; it brings robbers to arrive.
Fourth Six: waiting in blood; coming out from the pit.
Fifth Nine: waiting amid wine and food; constancy is good fortune.
Top Six: entering the pit; three uninvited guests come. Receive them with rever-
ence; in the end good fortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Waiting may be read as a pattern of action rather than a detached
prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure govern suc-
cess or danger.
Xu: there is trust; luminous success. Constancy is good fortune; favorable to cross
the great river.
Initial Nine: waiting in the outskirts; favorable to use constancy; no blame attaches.
Second Nine: waiting on the sand; some small words, yet finally good fortune.
Third Nine: waiting in the mud; it brings robbers to arrive.
Fourth Six: waiting in blood; coming out from the pit.
Fifth Nine: waiting amid wine and food; constancy is good fortune.
Top Six: entering the pit; three uninvited guests come. Receive them with rever-
ence; in the end good fortune.
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Xu: there is trust; luminous success. Constancy is good fortune; favorable to cross
the great river.
Initial Nine: waiting in the outskirts; favorable to use constancy; no blame attaches.

19
Second Nine: waiting on the sand; some small words, yet finally good fortune.
Third Nine: waiting in the mud; it brings robbers to arrive.
Fourth Six: waiting in blood; coming out from the pit.
Fifth Nine: waiting amid wine and food; constancy is good fortune.
Top Six: entering the pit; three uninvited guests come. Receive them with rever-
ence; in the end good fortune.

中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排
印，标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。卦名保留拼音Xu，英文标题“Waiting”

为no blame attaches， 不作 “没有问题” 的泛化说法。 “有孚” 译作there is trust/sincerity，
指内在可信之实，不只是主观相信。 “涉大川”保留cross the great river的古典象，不改
写成undertake a big project，但在注释中说明为涉险任大事。 “吉”译为good fortune，
指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随机好运。

语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化

言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第6 卦
䷅ 讼 (Song)
Contention
原文
讼，有孚，窒惕，中吉，终凶。利见大人，不利涉大川。
初六，不永所事，小有言，终吉。
九二，不克讼，归而逋其邑，人三百户，无眚。
六三，食旧德，贞厉，终吉。或从王事，无成。
九四，不克讼，复即命渝，安贞吉。
九五，讼，元吉。
上九，或锡之鞶带，终朝三褫之。
关键词释义
卦名 讼（Song） ：争讼之局；重在止争、求中、戒惧与见大人裁断。
英译标题 Contention。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身
份。
讼 争讼；有孚而窒，故须戒惧止争。
中吉终凶 中道可吉，争到底则凶。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
利见大人 宜亲近、咨取或得见德位相称者，以定方向。
涉大川 涉险成事；指重大行动与跨越艰难处境。
大人 德位相称、能定大局者；英译作 the Great Person。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
20

21
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Song: there is trust, but it is blocked; be apprehensive. The middle is good fortune,
the end misfortune. Favorable to see the Great Person; not favorable to cross the
great river.
Initial Six: do not prolong the affair; there are small words, but the end is good
fortune.
Second Nine: unable to prevail in contention, he returns and hides in his town of
three hundred households; no disaster.
Third Six: feeding on old virtue; constancy is perilous, yet finally good fortune. If
following the king’s affairs, claim no achievement.
Fourth Nine: unable to prevail in contention, he returns to command and changes
course; peaceful constancy is good fortune.
Fifth Nine: contention; greatly good fortune.
Top Nine: one may be bestowed a ceremonial belt, yet by morning it is stripped
away three times.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Contention may be read as a pattern of action rather than a
detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Song: there is trust, but it is blocked; be apprehensive. The middle is good fortune,
the end misfortune. Favorable to see the Great Person; not favorable to cross the
great river.

22 第6 卦
Initial Six: do not prolong the affair; there are small words, but the end is good
fortune.
Second Nine: unable to prevail in contention, he returns and hides in his town of
three hundred households; no disaster.
Third Six: feeding on old virtue; constancy is perilous, yet finally good fortune. If
following the king’s affairs, claim no achievement.
Fourth Nine: unable to prevail in contention, he returns to command and changes
course; peaceful constancy is good fortune.
Fifth Nine: contention; greatly good fortune.
Top Nine: one may be bestowed a ceremonial belt, yet by morning it is stripped
away three times.
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Song: there is trust, but it is blocked; be apprehensive. The middle is good fortune,
the end misfortune. Favorable to see the Great Person; not favorable to cross the
great river.
Initial Six: do not prolong the affair; there are small words, but the end is good
fortune.
Second Nine: unable to prevail in contention, he returns and hides in his town of
three hundred households; no disaster.
Third Six: feeding on old virtue; constancy is perilous, yet finally good fortune. If
following the king’s affairs, claim no achievement.
Fourth Nine: unable to prevail in contention, he returns to command and changes
course; peaceful constancy is good fortune.
Fifth Nine: contention; greatly good fortune.
Top Nine: one may be bestowed a ceremonial belt, yet by morning it is stripped
away three times.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Song is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Con-
tention, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the origi-
nal term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the
Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an
English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across
all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divina-
tion or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.

23
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排印，
标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。 卦名保留拼音Song， 英文标题 “Contention”
只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“讼”不作一般quarrel，而作contention/litigation； “中吉终凶”译出适可而
止与穷争之戒。
术语取舍。“贞吉”译作constancy brings good fortune， 强调吉由守正而来。 “有孚”译作
there is trust/sincerity，指内在可信之实，不只是主观相信。 “利见大人”译作favorable
to see/behold the Great Person，既保留见贤取法，也保留政治伦理中的定向作用。 “涉
大川”保留cross the great river的古典象，不改写成undertake a big project，但在注
释中说明为涉险任大事。 “厉”译为peril，不等同于 misfortune；它提示戒惧而非判定
终局。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随机好运。 “凶”译为
misfortune，指行为与时位相违所趋向的败坏或危险。 “大人”译为the Great Person，指
德位相称、足以定向共同体者，不是普通重要人物。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第7 卦
䷆ 师 (Shi)
The Army
原文
师，贞，丈人吉，无咎。
初六，师出以律，否臧凶。
九二，在师中吉，无咎，王三锡命。
六三，师或舆尸，凶。
六四，师左次，无咎。
六五，田有禽，利执言，无咎。长子帅师，弟子舆尸，贞凶。
上六，大君有命，开国承家，小人勿用。
关键词释义
卦名 师（Shi） ：众与军；强调纪律、正当性、成熟统率与不用小人。
英译标题 The Army。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
师 众也、军也；动众须正。
丈人 老成有德之统率者。
律 纪律与名义。
贞凶 虽持守而所守失时或失位，故成凶。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
小人 德量狭小、不能承担公义者；不仅指社会地位卑微者。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
24

25
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Shi: constancy; an elder leader is good fortune. No blame attaches.
Initial Six: the army goes forth by discipline; if not well ordered, misfortune.
Second Nine: in the center of the army, good fortune and without blame; the king
grants command three times.
Third Six: the army may carry corpses in wagons; misfortune.
Fourth Six: the army camps to the left; no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: there is game in the field; favorable to hold the word. No blame attaches.
The elder son leads the army; lesser sons carry corpses. Though steadfast, misfor-
tune.
Top Six: the great ruler has command; open states and sustain houses. Do not em-
ploy small persons.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, The Army may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.
Shi: constancy; an elder leader is good fortune. no blame attaches.
Initial Six: the army goes forth by discipline; if not well ordered, misfortune.
Second Nine: in the center of the army, good fortune and without blame; the king
grants command three times.
Third Six: the army may carry corpses in wagons; misfortune.
Fourth Six: the army camps to the left; no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: there is game in the field; favorable to hold the word. no blame attaches.
The elder son leads the army; lesser sons carry corpses. Though steadfast, misfor-
tune.
Top Six: the great ruler has command; open states and sustain houses. Do not em-
ploy small persons.

The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the Great

本卦义例。“师”兼军旅与众，译为The Army，但说明其核心在纪律与丈人之正，不鼓吹

第8 卦
䷇ 比 (Bi)
Holding Together
原文
比，吉。原筮元永贞，无咎。不宁方来，后夫凶。
初六，有孚比之，无咎。有孚盈缶，终来有它吉。
六二，比之自内，贞吉。
六三，比之匪人。
六四，外比之，贞吉。
九五，显比，王用三驱，失前禽。邑人不诫，吉。
上六，比之无首，凶。
关键词释义
卦名 比（Bi） ：亲比相附；重在信实结盟、及时归附与所比得正。
英译标题 Holding Together。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留
专名身份。
比 亲比、相附；须以诚信为本。
原筮 再审其本，确认所比是否元永贞。
后夫 迟疑不决而后至者。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
28

29
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Bi: good fortune. Re-examine the divination: originary, enduring, steadfast; no
blame attaches. The unsettled come; the latecomer is misfortune.
Initial Six: with trust, hold together with them; no blame attaches. Trust fills the
earthen vessel; in the end other good fortune comes.
Second Six: holding together from within; constancy is good fortune.
Third Six: holding together with the wrong people.
Fourth Six: holding together outwardly; constancy is good fortune.
Fifth Nine: manifest union. The king uses the three-sided hunt and lets the forward
game escape. The townspeople are not warned; good fortune.
Top Six: holding together without a head; misfortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Holding Together may be read as a pattern of action rather than
a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Bi: good fortune. Re-examine the divination: originary, enduring, steadfast; no
blame attaches. The unsettled come; the latecomer is misfortune.
Initial Six: with trust, hold together with them; no blame attaches. Trust fills the
earthen vessel; in the end other good fortune comes.
Second Six: holding together from within; constancy is good fortune.
Third Six: holding together with the wrong people.
Fourth Six: holding together outwardly; constancy is good fortune.
Fifth Nine: manifest union. The king uses the three-sided hunt and lets the forward
game escape. The townspeople are not warned; good fortune.
Top Six: holding together without a head; misfortune.

第9 卦
䷈ 小畜 (Xiao Xu)
Small Accumulation
原文
小畜，亨。密云不雨，自我西郊。
初九，复自道，何其咎？吉。
九二，牵复，吉。
九三，舆说辐，夫妻反目。
六四，有孚，血去惕出，无咎。
九五，有孚挛如，富以其邻。
上九，既雨既处，尚德载，妇贞厉。月几望，君子征凶。
关键词释义
卦名 小畜（Xiao Xu） ：小有所蓄；以柔制刚，云密未雨，势未大成。
英译标题 Small Accumulation。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保
留专名身份。
小畜 小有畜止；柔力蓄刚而未能大成。
密云不雨 势已聚而功未成。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
31

32 第9 卦
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Xiao Xu: through-going. Dense clouds but no rain, coming from our western out-
skirts.
Initial Nine: returning by one’s own path; what blame is there? Good fortune.
Second Nine: drawn back in return; good fortune.
Third Nine: the wagon loses its spokes; husband and wife turn eyes against each
other.
Fourth Six: there is trust; blood departs and fear goes out. No blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: trust binds closely; rich together with the neighbor.
Top Nine: rain has fallen and things are settled; virtue is esteemed and borne. For a
woman, constancy is perilous. The moon nearly full; for the noble one, to campaign
is misfortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Small Accumulation may be read as a pattern of action rather
than a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral mea-
sure govern success or danger.

skirts.

Second Nine: drawn back in return; good fortune.
Third Nine: the wagon loses its spokes; husband and wife turn eyes against each
other.
Fourth Six: there is trust; blood departs and fear goes out. no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: trust binds closely; rich together with the neighbor.
Top Nine: rain has fallen and things are settled; virtue is esteemed and borne. For a
woman, constancy is perilous. The moon nearly full; for the noble one, to campaign
is misfortune.

中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、卦名、卦辞、爻位与爻辞逐项校入；本终校本采用简
体排印，标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。卦名保留拼音 Xiao Xu，英文标题
“Small Accumulation”只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“密云不雨”保留蓄势未成之象，避免解释成天气预报。
术语取舍。“无咎”统一为no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “有孚”译
作 there is trust/sincerity，指内在可信之实，不只是主观相信。 “征”按主动推进、出行
或征伐译出，随卦爻语境在set forth / campaign / go forth间取舍。 “厉”译为peril，不
等同于 misfortune；它提示戒惧而非判定终局。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的
处境判断，不等于随机好运。 “凶”译为misfortune，指行为与时位相违所趋向的败坏或
危险。 “君子”译为the noble one，指修德成位者，避免 gentleman 的阶级和社交色彩。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。

34 第9 卦
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第10 卦
䷉ 履 (Lu)
Treading
原文
履虎尾，不咥人，亨。
初九，素履，往，无咎。
九二，履道坦坦，幽人贞吉。
六三，眇能视，跛能履。履虎尾，咥人，凶。武人为于大君。
九四，履虎尾，愬愬，终吉。
九五，夬履，贞厉。
上九，视履，考祥其旋，元吉。
关键词释义
卦名 履（Lu） ：履行礼节；如履虎尾，重在敬慎、礼度与进退分寸。
英译标题 Treading。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
履 践履、礼行；处危而以礼度通。
虎尾 危险临身之象。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
35

36 第10 卦
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Lu: treading on the tiger’s tail; it does not bite the person. Through-going.
Initial Nine: plain treading; to go, no blame attaches.
Second Nine: treading a level path; for the secluded person, constancy is good for-
tune.
Third Six: the one-eyed can see, the lame can tread. Treading on the tiger’s tail, it
bites the person; misfortune. A warrior acts for the great ruler.
Fourth Nine: treading on the tiger’s tail, fearful and cautious; finally good fortune.
Fifth Nine: resolute treading; constancy is perilous.
Top Nine: observe the treading and examine the signs of return; greatly good for-
tune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Treading may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.
Lu: treading on the tiger’s tail; it does not bite the person. Through-going.
Initial Nine: plain treading; to go, no blame attaches.
Second Nine: treading a level path; for the secluded person, constancy is good for-
tune.
Third Six: the one-eyed can see, the lame can tread. Treading on the tiger’s tail, it
bites the person; misfortune. A warrior acts for the great ruler.
Fourth Nine: treading on the tiger’s tail, fearful and cautious; finally good fortune.
Fifth Nine: resolute treading; constancy is perilous.
Top Nine: observe the treading and examine the signs of return; greatly good for-
tune.

37
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Lu: treading on the tiger’s tail; it does not bite the person. Through-going.
Initial Nine: plain treading; to go, no blame attaches.
Second Nine: treading a level path; for the secluded person, constancy is good for-
tune.
Third Six: the one-eyed can see, the lame can tread. Treading on the tiger’s tail, it
bites the person; misfortune. A warrior acts for the great ruler.
Fourth Nine: treading on the tiger’s tail, fearful and cautious; finally good fortune.
Fifth Nine: resolute treading; constancy is perilous.
Top Nine: observe the treading and examine the signs of return; greatly good for-
tune.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Lu is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Treading,
is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the original term.
The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the Great
Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an English
reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across all sixty-
four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divination
or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排
印， 标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。 卦名保留拼音Lu， 英文标题“Treading”
只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“履虎尾”按礼行于险境处理，treading 保留践履与礼度双义。
术语取舍。“贞吉”译作constancy brings good fortune，强调吉由守正而来。 “无咎”统
一为 no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “往”译为go / set out，说明
其可否取决于时位，不等于一般行动自由。 “厉”译为peril，不等同于misfortune；它提
示戒惧而非判定终局。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随机好
运。 “凶”译为misfortune，指行为与时位相违所趋向的败坏或危险。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第11 卦
䷊ 泰 (Tai)
Peace
原文
泰，小往大来，吉亨。
初九，拔茅茹，以其汇，征吉。
九二，包荒，用冯河，不遐遗，朋亡，得尚于中行。
九三，无平不陂，无往不复。艰贞，无咎。勿恤其孚，于食有福。
六四，翩翩，不富以其邻，不戒以孚。
六五，帝乙归妹，以祉元吉。
上六，城复于隍，勿用师。自邑告命，贞吝。
关键词释义
卦名 泰（Tai） ：天地交而万物通；小往大来，象征通泰与守成之戒。
英译标题 Peace。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
泰 通泰；天地交而上下通。
小往大来 阴小退而阳大来，象通泰之势。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
38

39
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Tai: the small goes, the great comes; good fortune and through-going.
Initial Nine: pulling up grass with its roots, joined with its kind; to campaign is good
fortune.
Second Nine: embracing the uncultivated; crossing the river without a boat; not
leaving the distant behind; losing private companions, one attains honor in the mid-
dle way.
Third Nine: no level ground without slope, no going without return. Difficult con-
stancy; no blame attaches. Do not worry over trust; in food there is blessing.
Fourth Six: fluttering down; not rich, yet with neighbors; not warned, yet by trust.
Fifth Six: Di Yi gives his younger sister in marriage; with blessing, greatly good for-
tune.
Top Six: the city wall falls back into the moat; do not use the army. Announce com-
mands from one’s own town; constancy brings regret.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Peace may be read as a pattern of action rather than a detached
prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure govern suc-
cess or danger.

fortune.

leaving the distant behind; losing private companions, one attains honor in the mid-
dle way.
Third Nine: no level ground without slope, no going without return. Difficult con-
stancy; no blame attaches. Do not worry over trust; in food there is blessing.
Fourth Six: fluttering down; not rich, yet with neighbors; not warned, yet by trust.
Fifth Six: Di Yi gives his younger sister in marriage; with blessing, greatly good
fortune.

40 第11 卦
Top Six: the city wall falls back into the moat; do not use the army. Announce com-
mands from one’s own town; constancy brings regret.

只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“小往大来”按阴阳消长与上下交通解释，peace 不是静止和平，而是通泰。

动推进、出行或征伐译出，随卦爻语境在set forth / campaign / go forth间取舍。 “往”译
为go / set out，说明其可否取决于时位，不等于一般行动自由。 “吝”译为regret / shame

第12 卦
䷋ 否 (Pi)
Obstruction
原文
否之匪人，不利君子贞，大往小来。
初六，拔茅茹，以其汇，贞吉，亨。
六二，包承，小人吉，大人否亨。
六三，包羞。
九四，有命无咎，畴离祉。
九五，休否，大人吉。其亡其亡，系于苞桑。
上九，倾否，先否后喜。
关键词释义
卦名 否（Pi） ：天地不交而闭塞；大往小来，君子处否而守正。
英译标题 Obstruction。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身
份。
否 闭塞；天地不交，人道不通。
匪人 非其人、非人道之类，示道闭于邪。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
大人 德位相称、能定大局者；英译作 the Great Person。
小人 德量狭小、不能承担公义者；不仅指社会地位卑微者。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
42

43
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Pi: obstruction by non-persons; not favorable for the noble one’s constancy. The
great goes, the small comes.
Initial Six: pulling up grass with its roots, joined with its kind; constancy is good
fortune and through-going.
Second Six: embracing and bearing; good fortune for the small person. The Great
Person is obstructed yet succeeds.
Third Six: embracing shame.
Fourth Nine: there is mandate; no blame attaches. Those of one’s kind share the
blessing.
Fifth Nine: obstruction comes to rest; good fortune for the Great Person.“It may
perish, it may perish!”- tied to a clump of mulberry.
Top Nine: overturning obstruction; first blocked, afterward joy.
面向英语母语者的自然意译

detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.

fortune and through-going.
Second Six: embracing and bearing; good fortune for the small person. The Great
Person is obstructed yet succeeds.
Third Six: embracing shame.

Fourth Nine: there is mandate; no blame attaches. Those of one’s kind share the
blessing.
Fifth Nine: obstruction comes to rest; good fortune for the Great Person.“It may
perish, it may perish!”- tied to a clump of mulberry.
Top Nine: overturning obstruction; first blocked, afterward joy.

第13 卦
䷌ 同人 (Tong Ren)
Fellowship with Others
原文
同人于野，亨。利涉大川，利君子贞。
初九，同人于门，无咎。
六二，同人于宗，吝。
九三，伏戎于莽，升其高陵，三岁不兴。
九四，乘其墉，弗克攻，吉。
九五，同人，先号咷而后笑，大师克相遇。
上九，同人于郊，无悔。
关键词释义
卦名 同人（Tong Ren） ：与人同道；由宗族私合推向郊野公同。
英译标题 Fellowship with Others。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音
保留专名身份。
同人 与人同道；由私门出于郊野之公。
于野 在郊野，示公同而非私党。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
涉大川 涉险成事；指重大行动与跨越艰难处境。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
46

47
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Fellowship with others in the open field; through-going. Favorable to cross the great
river; favorable for the noble one’s constancy.
Initial Nine: fellowship at the gate; no blame attaches.
Second Six: fellowship within the clan; regret.
Third Nine: hiding arms in the thicket, climbing the high mound; for three years no
rising.
Fourth Nine: mounting the city wall, yet unable to attack; good fortune.
Fifth Nine: fellowship; first wailing, afterward laughter. Great armies overcome
and meet.
Top Nine: fellowship in the outskirts; no regret.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Fellowship with Others may be read as a pattern of action rather
than a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral mea-
sure govern success or danger.
Fellowship with others in the open field; through-going. Favorable to cross the great
river; favorable for the noble one’s constancy.
Initial Nine: fellowship at the gate; no blame attaches.
Second Six: fellowship within the clan; regret.
Third Nine: hiding arms in the thicket, climbing the high mound; for three years no
rising.
Fourth Nine: mounting the city wall, yet unable to attack; good fortune.
Fifth Nine: fellowship; first wailing, afterward laughter. Great armies overcome
and meet.
Top Nine: fellowship in the outskirts; no regret.

48 第13 卦
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Fellowship with others in the open field; through-going. Favorable to cross the great
river; favorable for the noble one’s constancy.
Initial Nine: fellowship at the gate; no blame attaches.
Second Six: fellowship within the clan; regret.
Third Nine: hiding arms in the thicket, climbing the high mound; for three years no
rising.
Fourth Nine: mounting the city wall, yet unable to attack; good fortune.
Fifth Nine: fellowship; first wailing, afterward laughter. Great armies overcome
and meet.
Top Nine: fellowship in the outskirts; no regret.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Tong Ren is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Fel-
lowship with Others, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for
the original term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble
one, the Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so
that an English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes
across all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical
divination or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image,
timing, position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、卦名、卦辞、爻位与爻辞逐项校入；本终校本采用简
体排印，标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。卦名保留拼音Tong Ren，英文标题
“Fellowship with Others”只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“同人于野”强调由私门出于公共场域，union 不作私人结党。
术语取舍。“无咎”统一为no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “涉大川”
保留cross the great river的古典象，不改写成undertake a big project，但在注释中说
明为涉险任大事。 “悔”译为regret，取可反省、可转圜之悔，不作最终灾祸。 “吝”译为
regret / shame / distress according to context，重在窘迫与可羞之迹。 “吉”译为good
fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随机好运。 “君子”译为the noble one，指修德
成位者，避免 gentleman 的阶级和社交色彩。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。

49
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第14 卦
䷍ 大有 (Da You)
Great Possession
原文
大有，元亨。
初九，无交害，匪咎，艰则无咎。
九二，大车以载，有攸往，无咎。
九三，公用亨于天子，小人弗克。
九四，匪其彭，无咎。
六五，厥孚交如，威如，吉。
上九，自天祐之，吉，无不利。
关键词释义
卦名 大有（Da You） ：大有其德与其位；重在有而不骄、富而能正。
英译标题 Great Possession。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专
名身份。
大有 大有其德与其位；富有须以明德节制。
元亨 元而能通，表示大端已具而其道可行。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
小人 德量狭小、不能承担公义者；不仅指社会地位卑微者。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
50

51
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Great Possession: originary and through-going.
Initial Nine: no harmful entanglement; this is not a fault. In difficulty, no blame
attaches.
Second Nine: a great cart for carrying; having somewhere to go, no blame attaches.
Third Nine: a duke makes offering to the Son of Heaven; a small person cannot do
this.
Fourth Nine: not relying on its abundance; no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: his trust is reciprocal and dignified; good fortune.
Top Nine: helped by Heaven; good fortune, nothing unfavorable.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Great Possession may be read as a pattern of action rather than
a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Great Possession: primal and through-going.
Initial Nine: no harmful entanglement; this is not a fault. In difficulty, no blame
attaches.
Second Nine: a great cart for carrying; having somewhere to go, no blame attaches.
Third Nine: a duke makes offering to the Son of Heaven; a small person cannot do
this.
Fourth Nine: not relying on its abundance; no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: his trust is reciprocal and dignified; good fortune.
Top Nine: helped by Heaven; good fortune, nothing unfavorable.
最终推荐的深度文化译文

Initial Nine: no harmful entanglement; this is not a fault. In difficulty, no blame

第15 卦
䷎ 谦 (Qian)
Humility
原文
谦，亨，君子有终。
初六，谦谦君子，用涉大川，吉。
六二，鸣谦，贞吉。
九三，劳谦，君子有终，吉。
六四，无不利，㧑谦。
六五，不富以其邻，利用侵伐，无不利。
上六，鸣谦，利用行师，征邑国。
关键词释义
卦名 谦（Qian） ：以卑自牧；满而能下，故君子有终。
英译标题 Humility。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
谦 谦下自牧；德盛而处下。
有终 能守其终，不以满招损。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
涉大川 涉险成事；指重大行动与跨越艰难处境。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
53

54 第15 卦
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Humility: through-going. The noble one has completion.
Initial Six: humbly humble noble one; useful to cross the great river; good fortune.
Second Six: humility that sounds forth; constancy is good fortune.
Third Nine: laborious humility; the noble one has completion; good fortune.
Fourth Six: nothing unfavorable; extend humility.
Fifth Six: not rich, yet with neighbors; favorable to use punitive action; nothing un-
favorable.
Top Six: humility that sounds forth; favorable to send the army and campaign
against towns and states.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Humility may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.
Humility: through-going. The noble one has completion.

Second Six: humility that sounds forth; constancy is good fortune.
Third Nine: laborious humility; the noble one has completion; good fortune.
Fourth Six: nothing unfavorable; extend humility.
Fifth Six: not rich, yet with neighbors; favorable to use punitive action; nothing
unfavorable.
Top Six: humility that sounds forth; favorable to send the army and campaign
against towns and states.
最终推荐的深度文化译文

Initial Six: humbly humble noble one; useful to cross the great river; good fortune.
Second Six: humility that sounds forth; constancy is good fortune.

第16 卦
䷏ 豫 (Yu)
Enthusiasm
原文
豫，利建侯、行师。
初六，鸣豫，凶。
六二，介于石，不终日，贞吉。
六三，盱豫，悔，迟有悔。
九四，由豫，大有得。勿疑，朋盍簪。
六五，贞疾，恒不死。
上六，冥豫，成有渝，无咎。
关键词释义
卦名 豫（Yu） ：悦豫与预备；能动众，也可能流于逸乐。
英译标题 Enthusiasm。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身
份。
豫 悦豫与预备；可动众，亦须防逸乐。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
侯 侯伯之位；多指新秩序建立时的分封、任命与组织化。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
56

57
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Enthusiasm: favorable to establish lords and send the army.
Initial Six: sounding forth in enthusiasm; misfortune.
Second Six: firm as stone; not waiting till the day ends; constancy brings good for-
tune.
Third Six: looking upward in enthusiasm; regret. Delay brings regret.
Fourth Nine: from this enthusiasm, great gain. Do not doubt; friends gather like
hair bound by a clasp.
Fifth Six: steadfast in illness; enduring, not dying.
Top Six: darkened enthusiasm; when completion changes, no blame attaches.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Enthusiasm may be read as a pattern of action rather than a
detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.

Second Six: firm as stone; not waiting till the day ends; constancy brings good for-

Fourth Nine: from this enthusiasm, great gain. Do not doubt; friends gather like
hair bound by a clasp.
Fifth Six: steadfast in illness; enduring, not dying.
Top Six: darkened enthusiasm; when completion changes, no blame attaches.

言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第17 卦
䷐ 随 (Sui)
Following
原文
随，元亨利贞，无咎。
初九，官有渝，贞吉。出门交有功。
六二，系小子，失丈夫。
六三，系丈夫，失小子。随有求得，利居贞。
九四，随有获，贞凶。有孚在道以明，何咎？
九五，孚于嘉，吉。
上六，拘系之，乃从维之，王用亨于西山。
关键词释义
卦名 随（Sui） ：随时而从；贵在所随得正，不为私欲牵引。
英译标题 Following。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
随 随时从正；所随不正则失其道。
元亨利贞 四德并举：创始、通达、合宜、正固，构成《易》之基本价值序列。
元亨 元而能通，表示大端已具而其道可行。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
贞凶 虽持守而所守失时或失位，故成凶。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
59

60 第17 卦
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Following: originary, through-going, favorable, steadfast; no blame attaches.
Initial Nine: the office changes; constancy brings good fortune. Going out the gate
and associating brings merit.
Second Six: bound to the little child, losing the mature man.
Third Six: bound to the mature man, losing the little child. In following, what is
sought is gained; favorable to dwell in constancy.
Fourth Nine: following and gaining; constancy is misfortune. With trust on the way
and clarity, what blame?
Fifth Nine: trust in what is excellent; good fortune.
Top Six: bound and tied, then further fastened. The king uses this to make offering
on the western mountain.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Following may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.
Following: primal, through-going, favorable, and constant; no blame attaches.
Initial Nine: the office changes; constancy brings good fortune. Going out the gate
and associating brings merit.
Second Six: bound to the little child, losing the mature man.
Third Six: bound to the mature man, losing the little child. In following, what is
sought is gained; favorable to dwell in constancy.

61
Fourth Nine: following and gaining; constancy is misfortune. With trust on the way
and clarity, what blame?
Fifth Nine: trust in what is excellent; good fortune.
Top Six: bound and tied, then further fastened. The king uses this to make offering
on the western mountain.
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Following: primal, through-going, favorable, and constant; no blame attaches.
Initial Nine: the office changes; constancy brings good fortune. Going out the gate
and associating brings merit.
Second Six: bound to the little child, losing the mature man.
Third Six: bound to the mature man, losing the little child. In following, what is
sought is gained; favorable to dwell in constancy.
Fourth Nine: following and gaining; constancy is misfortune. With trust on the way
and clarity, what blame?
Fifth Nine: trust in what is excellent; good fortune.
Top Six: bound and tied, then further fastened. The king uses this to make offering
on the western mountain.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Sui is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Following,
is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the original term.
The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the Great
Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an English
reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across all sixty-
four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divination
or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排
印， 标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。 卦名保留拼音Sui， 英文标题 “Following”
只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“随”是随时从正，不是盲从；译文用 Following 并补充德性方向。
术语取舍。“元亨利贞”不拆成四个互不相干的吉祥词，而按创始、通达、合宜、正固的义
理序列处理。 “元亨”译作primal/originary and through-going，保留“大端可通”之
义。“利贞”译为favorable through constancy，不译成 profitable divination。“贞

62 第17 卦
吉”译作constancy brings good fortune，强调吉由守正而来。 “无咎”统一为no blame
attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “有孚”译作there is trust/sincerity，指内在
可信之实，不只是主观相信。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随
机好运。 “凶”译为misfortune，指行为与时位相违所趋向的败坏或危险。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第18 卦
䷑ 蛊 (Gu)
Correcting Decay
原文
蛊，元亨，利涉大川。先甲三日，后甲三日。
初六，干父之蛊。有子，考无咎，厉，终吉。
九二，干母之蛊，不可贞。
九三，干父之蛊，小有悔，无大咎。
六四，裕父之蛊，往见吝。
六五，干父之蛊，用誉。
上九，不事王侯，高尚其事。
关键词释义
卦名 蛊（Gu） ：积弊败坏之后的整治；含继承、改革与承责之义。
英译标题 Correcting Decay。标题取意译， 以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专
名身份。
蛊 坏败之事；重在整饬积弊。
先甲后甲 变革前后皆须审度。
元亨 元而能通，表示大端已具而其道可行。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
涉大川 涉险成事；指重大行动与跨越艰难处境。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
侯 侯伯之位；多指新秩序建立时的分封、任命与组织化。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
63

64 第18 卦
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Gu: originary and through-going; favorable to cross the great river. Three days
before Jia, three days after Jia.
Initial Six: dealing with the father’s decay. With a son, the deceased father has no
blame attaches. Perilous, yet finally good fortune.
Second Nine: dealing with the mother’s decay; one cannot be rigidly steadfast.
Third Nine: dealing with the father’s decay; small regret, no great blame.
Fourth Six: indulging the father’s decay; to go brings regret.
Fifth Six: dealing with the father’s decay; use brings praise.
Top Nine: not serving kings and lords; he holds his own affairs high.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Correcting Decay may be read as a pattern of action rather than
a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Gu: primal and through-going; favorable to cross the great river. Three days before
Jia, three days after Jia.
Initial Six: dealing with the father’s decay. With a son, the deceased father has no
blame attaches. Perilous, yet finally good fortune.
Second Nine: dealing with the mother’s decay; one cannot be rigidly steadfast.
Third Nine: dealing with the father’s decay; small regret, no great blame.

65
Fourth Six: indulging the father’s decay; to go brings regret.
Fifth Six: dealing with the father’s decay; use brings praise.
Top Nine: not serving kings and lords; he holds his own affairs high.
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Gu: primal and through-going; favorable to cross the great river. Three days before
Jia, three days after Jia.
Initial Six: dealing with the father’s decay. With a son, the deceased father has no
blame attaches. Perilous, yet finally good fortune.
Second Nine: dealing with the mother’s decay; one cannot be rigidly steadfast.
Third Nine: dealing with the father’s decay; small regret, no great blame.

English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Gu is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Correcting
Decay, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the original
term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the
Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an
English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across
all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divina-
tion or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排
印， 标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。 卦名保留拼音Gu， 英文标题 “Correcting
Decay”只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“蛊”取败坏后整饬之义，Correcting Decay较Gu as poison更适合跨文化读
者。
术语取舍。“元亨” 译作primal/originary and through-going， 保留 “大端可通” 之义。 “无
咎”统一为no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “涉大川”保留cross the
great river的古典象，不改写成 undertake a big project，但在注释中说明为涉险任大
事。 “往” 译为go / set out， 说明其可否取决于时位， 不等于一般行动自由。 “悔” 译为regret，
取可反省、可转圜之悔，不作最终灾祸。 “吝”译为regret / shame / distress according

66 第18 卦
to context，重在窘迫与可羞之迹。 “厉”译为peril，不等同于misfortune；它提示戒惧
而非判定终局。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随机好运。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母

言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第19 卦
䷒ 临 (Lin)
Approach
原文
临，元亨利贞，至于八月有凶。
初九，咸临，贞吉。
九二，咸临，吉，无不利。
六三，甘临，无攸利，既忧之，无咎。
六四，至临，无咎。
六五，知临，大君之宜，吉。
上六，敦临，吉，无咎。
关键词释义
卦名 临（Lin） ：上临下、德泽将至；盛长之中已含衰退之戒。
英译标题 Approach。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
临 上临下、德泽将至。
八月有凶 盛长之时已含衰退之戒。
元亨利贞 四德并举：创始、通达、合宜、正固，构成《易》之基本价值序列。
元亨 元而能通，表示大端已具而其道可行。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
67

68 第19 卦
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Approach: originary, through-going, favorable, steadfast; when the eighth month
comes, there is misfortune.
Initial Nine: jointly approaching; constancy brings good fortune.
Second Nine: jointly approaching; good fortune, nothing unfavorable.
Third Six: sweet approach; nothing is favorable. Once worried over it, no blame
attaches.
Fourth Six: arriving approach; no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: wise approach; fitting for the great ruler; good fortune.
Top Six: generous approach; good fortune, no blame attaches.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Approach may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.

comes, there is misfortune.
Initial Nine: jointly approaching; constancy brings good fortune.
Second Nine: jointly approaching; good fortune, nothing unfavorable.
Third Six: sweet approach; nothing is favorable. Once worried over it, no blame
attaches.
Fourth Six: arriving approach; no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: wise approach; fitting for the great ruler; good fortune.
Top Six: generous approach; good fortune, no blame attaches.

第20 卦
䷓ 观 (Guan)
Contemplation
原文
观，盥而不荐，有孚颙若。
初六，童观，小人无咎，君子吝。
六二，闚观，利女贞。
六三，观我生，进退。
六四，观国之光，利用宾于王。
九五，观我生，君子无咎。
上九，观其生，君子无咎。
关键词释义
卦名 观（Guan） ：观示与观省；礼未荐而诚已显，亦指被观与自观。
英译标题 Contemplation。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名
身份。
观 观示与观省；人观我，我亦观己。
盥而不荐 礼未完成而诚敬已见。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
小人 德量狭小、不能承担公义者；不仅指社会地位卑微者。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
70

71
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Contemplation: hands washed but offerings not yet presented; there is trust, solemn
and uplifted.
Initial Six: childish viewing; no blame for the small person, regret for the noble one.
Second Six: peeping contemplation; favorable for a woman’s constancy.
Third Six: contemplating my own life-course; advance or withdraw.
Fourth Six: contemplating the glory of the state; favorable to be a guest of the king.
Fifth Nine: contemplating my own life-course; the noble one has no blame attaches.
Top Nine: contemplating another’s life-course; the noble one has no blame attaches.

a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.

Top Nine: contemplating another’s life-course; the noble one has no blame attaches.

across all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical
divination or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image,
timing, position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、卦名、卦辞、爻位与爻辞逐项校入；本终校本采用简体
排印，标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。卦名保留拼音Guan，英文标题“Con-
templation”只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“盥而不荐”译出祭礼未竟而诚敬已显，保留 ritual suspense。
术语取舍。“无咎”统一为no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “有孚”译
作there is trust/sincerity， 指内在可信之实， 不只是主观相信。 “吝”译为regret / shame
/ distress according to context，重在窘迫与可羞之迹。 “君子”译为the noble one，指
修德成位者，避免gentleman 的阶级和社交色彩。 “小人”译为the small person，指德
量狭小者，不简单等同社会身份低者。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第21 卦
䷔ 噬嗑 (Shi He)
Biting Through
原文
噬嗑，亨，利用狱。
初九，屦校灭趾，无咎。
六二，噬肤灭鼻，无咎。
六三，噬腊肉，遇毒。小吝，无咎。
九四，噬乾胏，得金矢。利艰贞，吉。
六五，噬乾肉，得黄金。贞厉，无咎。
上九，何校灭耳，凶。
关键词释义
卦名 噬嗑（Shi He） ：咬合而去间；象征刑罚、决断与去除阻隔。
英译标题 Biting Through。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专
名身份。
噬嗑 咬合去间；以刑罚决断除阻。
狱 刑狱与裁断，须中正。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
73

74 第21 卦
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Biting Through: through-going; favorable to use legal judgment.
Initial Nine: feet in stocks, toes covered; no blame attaches.
Second Six: biting soft flesh, the nose covered; no blame attaches.
Third Six: biting dried meat and meeting poison; small regret, no blame attaches.
Fourth Nine: biting dried gristly meat and obtaining a metal arrow; favorable in
difficult constancy; good fortune.
Fifth Six: biting dried meat and obtaining yellow gold; constancy is perilous, no
blame attaches.
Top Nine: carrying a cangue that covers the ears; misfortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Biting Through may be read as a pattern of action rather than
a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Biting Through: through-going; favorable to use legal judgment.
Initial Nine: feet in stocks, toes covered; no blame attaches.
Second Six: biting soft flesh, the nose covered; no blame attaches.
Third Six: biting dried meat and meeting poison; small regret, no blame attaches.
Fourth Nine: biting dried gristly meat and obtaining a metal arrow; favorable in
difficult constancy; good fortune.
Fifth Six: biting dried meat and obtaining yellow gold; constancy is perilous, no
blame attaches.
Top Nine: carrying a cangue that covers the ears; misfortune.
最终推荐的深度文化译文

Initial Nine: feet in stocks, toes covered; no blame attaches.

75
Second Six: biting soft flesh, the nose covered; no blame attaches.
Third Six: biting dried meat and meeting poison; small regret, no blame attaches.
Fourth Nine: biting dried gristly meat and obtaining a metal arrow; favorable in
difficult constancy; good fortune.
Fifth Six: biting dried meat and obtaining yellow gold; constancy is perilous, no
blame attaches.
Top Nine: carrying a cangue that covers the ears; misfortune.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Shi He is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Biting
Through, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the origi-
nal term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the
Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an
English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across
all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divina-
tion or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排
印， 标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。卦名保留拼音Shi He， 英文标题“Biting
Through”只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“噬嗑”按咬合去间之象处理，legal constraints只是社会义之一端。
术语取舍。“无咎”统一为no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “吝”译为
regret / shame / distress according to context，重在窘迫与可羞之迹。 “厉”译为peril，
不等同于 misfortune；它提示戒惧而非判定终局。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成

三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母

译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第22 卦
䷕ 贲 (Bi)
Adornment
原文
贲，亨，小利有攸往。
初九，贲其趾，舍车而徒。
六二，贲其须。
九三，贲如濡如，永贞吉。
六四，贲如皤如，白马翰如，匪寇婚媾。
六五，贲于丘园，束帛戋戋。吝，终吉。
上九，白贲，无咎。
关键词释义
卦名 贲（Bi） ：文饰与质素的关系；文以成礼，不可胜质。
英译标题 Adornment。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身
份。
贲 文饰、文明之饰。
白贲 返于质素之美。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。

利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。

刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Adornment: through-going; slightly favorable to set out.
Initial Nine: adorning the toes; leaving the carriage and walking.
Second Six: adorning the beard.
Third Nine: adorned and moistened; enduring constancy is good fortune.
Fourth Six: adorned, yet white; the white horse seems winged. Not a robber, but a
suitor.
Fifth Six: adornment in hill and garden; bundles of silk are scanty. Regret, but
finally good fortune.
Top Nine: plain white adornment; no blame attaches.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Adornment may be read as a pattern of action rather than a
detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.

第23 卦
䷖ 剥 (Bo)
Stripping Away
原文
剥，不利有攸往。
初六，剥床以足，蔑贞凶。
六二，剥床以辨，蔑贞凶。
六三，剥之无咎。
六四，剥床以肤，凶。
六五，贯鱼，以宫人宠，无不利。
上九，硕果不食，君子得舆，小人剥庐。
关键词释义
卦名 剥（Bo） ：阳德剥落；宜止不宜进，守其宅而避其势。
英译标题 Stripping Away。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专
名身份。
剥 剥落、侵蚀；阳德被削，宜止不宜进。
贞凶 虽持守而所守失时或失位，故成凶。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
小人 德量狭小、不能承担公义者；不仅指社会地位卑微者。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
79

80 第23 卦
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Stripping Away: not favorable to set out.
Initial Six: stripping the bed by its legs; destroying constancy, misfortune.
Second Six: stripping the bed by its frame; destroying constancy, misfortune.
Third Six: stripping it; no blame attaches.
Fourth Six: stripping the bed to the skin; misfortune.
Fifth Six: a string of fish, favored through palace people; nothing unfavorable.
Top Nine: the large fruit is not eaten; the noble one gains a carriage, the small per-
son loses his hut.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Stripping Away may be read as a pattern of action rather than
a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.

Fourth Six: stripping the bed to the skin; misfortune.
Fifth Six: a string of fish, favored through palace people; nothing unfavorable.

第24 卦
䷗ 复 (Fu)
Return
原文
复，亨。出入无疾，朋来无咎。反复其道，七日来复，利有攸往。
初九，不远复，无只悔，元吉。
六二，休复，吉。
六三，频复，厉，无咎。
六四，中行独复。
六五，敦复，无悔。
上六，迷复，凶，有灾眚。用行师，终有大败。以其国君，凶，至于十年不克征。
关键词释义
卦名 复（Fu） ：一阳来复；返本复初，生机重返。
英译标题 Return。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
复 返回、复初；一阳来复，生机初回。
七日来复 循环反复之时数象。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
82

83
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Return: through-going. Going out and coming in without illness; friends come, no
blame attaches. Reversing and returning on the way; in seven days comes return.
Favorable to set out.
Initial Nine: returning before going far; no great regret; greatly good fortune.
Second Six: noble return; good fortune.
Third Six: repeated return; perilous, no blame attaches.
Fourth Six: walking in the middle, returning alone.
Fifth Six: generous return; no regret.
Top Six: confused return; misfortune, with disaster. Using it to send armies ends
in great defeat. For the ruler of the state, misfortune; for ten years he cannot cam-
paign.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Return may be read as a pattern of action rather than a detached
prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure govern suc-
cess or danger.
Return: through-going. Going out and coming in without illness; friends come, no
blame attaches. Reversing and returning on the way; in seven days comes return.
Favorable to set out.
Initial Nine: returning before going far; no great regret; greatly good fortune.
Second Six: noble return; good fortune.
Third Six: repeated return; perilous, no blame attaches.
Fourth Six: walking in the middle, returning alone.
Fifth Six: generous return; no regret.

84 第24 卦
Top Six: confused return; misfortune, with disaster. Using it to send armies ends
in great defeat. For the ruler of the state, misfortune; for ten years he cannot cam-
paign.
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Return: through-going. Going out and coming in without illness; friends come, no
blame attaches. Reversing and returning on the way; in seven days comes return.
Favorable to set out.
Initial Nine: returning before going far; no great regret; greatly good fortune.
Second Six: noble return; good fortune.
Third Six: repeated return; perilous, no blame attaches.
Fourth Six: walking in the middle, returning alone.
Fifth Six: generous return; no regret.
Top Six: confused return; misfortune, with disaster. Using it to send armies ends
in great defeat. For the ruler of the state, misfortune; for ten years he cannot cam-
paign.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Fu is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Return, is
a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the original term.
The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the Great
Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an English
reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across all sixty-
four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divination
or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、卦名、卦辞、爻位与爻辞逐项校入；本终校本采用简体
排印， 标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。 卦名保留拼音Fu， 英文标题“Return”
只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“复”译为 Return，强调一阳来复与循环回归，不作简单 reversal。
术语取舍。“无咎”统一为 no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “征”按
主动推进、出行或征伐译出，随卦爻语境在set forth / campaign / go forth间取舍。 “往”
译为go / set out，说明其可否取决于时位，不等于一般行动自由。 “悔”译为regret，取可
反省、可转圜之悔，不作最终灾祸。 “厉”译为peril，不等同于misfortune；它提示戒惧

85
而非判定终局。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随机好运。 “凶”
译为 misfortune，指行为与时位相违所趋向的败坏或危险。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第25 卦
䷘ 无妄 (Wu Wang)
Without Falsehood
原文
无妄，元亨利贞。其匪正有眚，不利有攸往。
初九，无妄，往吉。
六二，不耕获，不菑畬，则利有攸往。
六三，无妄之灾，或系之牛。行人之得，邑人之灾。
九四，可贞，无咎。
九五，无妄之疾，勿药有喜。
上九，无妄，行有眚，无攸利。
关键词释义
卦名 无妄（Wu Wang） ：不妄为、不虚伪；正则亨，失正则有眚。
英译标题 Without Falsehood。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留
专名身份。
无妄 不虚妄、不妄为。
眚 灾眚，因失正而生。
元亨利贞 四德并举：创始、通达、合宜、正固，构成《易》之基本价值序列。
元亨 元而能通，表示大端已具而其道可行。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
86

87
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Without Falsehood: originary, through-going, favorable, steadfast. If it is not right,
there is disaster; not favorable to set out.
Initial Nine: without falsehood; to go is good fortune.
Second Six: not plowing yet harvesting, not clearing yet reaping; then it is favorable
to set out.
Third Six: the disaster of no-falsehood: someone ties up an ox; the traveler gains it,
the townsman suffers.
Fourth Nine: one may be steadfast; no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: illness without falsehood; do not medicate, there will be joy.
Top Nine: without falsehood; action brings disaster, nothing is favorable.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Without Falsehood may be read as a pattern of action rather than
a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Without Falsehood: primal, through-going, favorable, and constant. If it is not right,
there is disaster; not favorable to set out.
Initial Nine: without falsehood; to go is good fortune.
Second Six: not plowing yet harvesting, not clearing yet reaping; then it is favorable
to set out.
Third Six: the disaster of no-falsehood: someone ties up an ox; the traveler gains it,
the townsman suffers.
Fourth Nine: one may be steadfast; no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: illness without falsehood; do not medicate, there will be joy.

88 第25 卦
Top Nine: without falsehood; action brings disaster, nothing is favorable.
最终推荐的深度文化译文

there is disaster; not favorable to set out.

第26 卦
䷙ 大畜 (Da Xu)
Great Accumulation
原文
大畜，利贞，不家食吉，利涉大川。
初九，有厉，利已。
九二，舆说輹。
九三，良马逐，利艰贞。曰闲舆卫，利有攸往。
六四，童牛之牿，元吉。
六五，豮豕之牙，吉。
上九，何天之衢，亨。
关键词释义
卦名 大畜（Da Xu） ：大者有所蓄；蓄德蓄才而后可行大事。
英译标题 Great Accumulation。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保
留专名身份。
大畜 大有所蓄；蓄德、蓄才、蓄势。
不家食 不私食于家，出而任事。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
涉大川 涉险成事；指重大行动与跨越艰难处境。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
90

91
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Great Accumulation: favorable to maintain constancy. Not eating at home is good
fortune; favorable to cross the great river.
Initial Nine: there is peril; favorable to stop.
Second Nine: the carriage loses its axle strap.
Third Nine: good horses pursue; favorable in difficult constancy. Daily practice
chariot and guard; favorable to set out.
Fourth Six: the young ox’s headboard; greatly good fortune.
Fifth Six: the tusk of a gelded boar; good fortune.
Top Nine: what a road of Heaven! Through-going.
面向英语母语者的自然意译

than a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral mea-
sure govern success or danger.

第27 卦
䷚ 颐 (Yi)
Nourishment
原文
颐贞吉，观颐，自求口实。
初九，舍尔灵龟，观我朵颐，凶。
六二，颠颐，拂经；于丘颐，征凶。
六三，拂颐，贞凶。十年勿用，无攸利。
六四，颠颐，吉。虎视眈眈，其欲逐逐，无咎。
六五，拂经，居贞吉，不可涉大川。
上九，由颐，厉吉，利涉大川。
关键词释义
卦名 颐（Yi） ：养口养德；观其所养与自养之道。
英译标题 Nourishment。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名
身份。
颐 养也；养口亦养德。
口实 饮食之实，亦指所养之道。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
贞凶 虽持守而所守失时或失位，故成凶。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
涉大川 涉险成事；指重大行动与跨越艰难处境。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
93

94 第27 卦
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Nourishment: constancy is good fortune. Observe nourishment; seek the substance
for one’s own mouth.
Initial Nine: leaving your numinous tortoise, you watch my jaws move; misfortune.
Second Six: inverted nourishment, contrary to the norm; seeking nourishment
from the hill, to campaign is misfortune.
Third Six: contrary nourishment; constancy misfortune. For ten years do not use
it; nothing is favorable.
Fourth Six: inverted nourishment; good fortune. The tiger watches intently, desire
pursuing; no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: contrary to the norm; to dwell in constancy brings good fortune. One can-
not cross the great river.
Top Nine: source of nourishment; perilous but good fortune. Favorable to cross the
great river.
