第28 卦
䷛ 大过 (Da Guo)
Great Exceeding
原文
大过，栋桡。利有攸往，亨。
初六，藉用白茅，无咎。
九二，枯杨生稊，老夫得其女妻，无不利。
九三，栋桡，凶。
九四，栋隆，吉，有它吝。
九五，枯杨生华，老妇得其士夫，无咎无誉。
上六，过涉灭顶，凶，无咎。
关键词释义
卦名 大过（Da Guo） ：大者过重；栋桡之象，须非常之处置。
英译标题 Great Exceeding。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专
名身份。
大过 大者过越、过重。
栋桡 栋梁挠曲，示结构承压。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
97

98 第28 卦
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Great Exceeding: the ridgepole bends. Favorable to set out; through-going.
Initial Six: using white rushes as padding; no blame attaches.
Second Nine: a withered poplar grows shoots; an old man gains a young wife; noth-
ing unfavorable.
Third Nine: the ridgepole bends; misfortune.
Fourth Nine: the ridgepole rises; good fortune, though other regret exists.
Fifth Nine: a withered poplar flowers; an old woman gains a young husband; no
blame, no praise.
Top Six: exceeding in crossing, submerged over the head; misfortune, yet no blame
attaches.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Great Exceeding may be read as a pattern of action rather than
a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Great Exceeding: the ridgepole bends. Favorable to set out; through-going.
Initial Six: using white rushes as padding; no blame attaches.
Second Nine: a withered poplar grows shoots; an old man gains a young wife; noth-
ing unfavorable.
Third Nine: the ridgepole bends; misfortune.
Fourth Nine: the ridgepole rises; good fortune, though other regret exists.
Fifth Nine: a withered poplar flowers; an old woman gains a young husband; no
blame attaches, no praise.
Top Six: exceeding in crossing, submerged over the head; misfortune, yet no blame
attaches.

99
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Great Exceeding: the ridgepole bends. Favorable to set out; through-going.
Initial Six: using white rushes as padding; no blame attaches.
Second Nine: a withered poplar grows shoots; an old man gains a young wife; noth-
ing unfavorable.
Third Nine: the ridgepole bends; misfortune.
Fourth Nine: the ridgepole rises; good fortune, though other regret exists.
Fifth Nine: a withered poplar flowers; an old woman gains a young husband; no
blame attaches, no praise.
Top Six: exceeding in crossing, submerged over the head; misfortune, yet no blame
attaches.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Da Guo is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Great
Exceeding, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the
original term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble
one, the Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so
that an English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes
across all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical
divination or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image,
timing, position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、卦名、卦辞、爻位与爻辞逐项校入；本终校本采用简
体排印，标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。卦名保留拼音 Da Guo，英文标题
“Great Exceeding”只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“大过”按结构过重、栋梁承压解释，Great Exceeding不是道德罪过。
术语取舍。“无咎”统一为no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “往”译为
go / set out，说明其可否取决于时位，不等于一般行动自由。 “吝”译为regret / shame /
distress according to context，重在窘迫与可羞之迹。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向
善成的处境判断，不等于随机好运。 “凶”译为misfortune，指行为与时位相违所趋向的
败坏或危险。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第29 卦
䷜ 坎 (Kan)
The Repeated Abyss
原文
习坎，有孚，维心亨，行有尚。
初六，习坎，入于坎窞，凶。
九二，坎有险，求小得。
六三，来之坎坎，险且枕。入于坎窞，勿用。
六四，樽酒，簋贰，用缶。纳约自牖，终无咎。
九五，坎不盈，只既平，无咎。
上六，系用徽𬙊，寘于丛棘。三岁不得，凶。
关键词释义
卦名 坎（Kan） ：重险之中守孚；心亨而行有尚。
英译标题 The Repeated Abyss。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保
留专名身份。
坎 险也；重险之中贵在守孚。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
100

101
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Repeated Abyss: there is trust; the heart alone succeeds. Action has honor.
Initial Six: repeated abyss, entering the pit within the pit; misfortune.
Second Nine: the abyss has danger; seeking small gains.
Third Six: coming and going through abyss upon abyss, perilous and blocked. En-
tering the pit within the pit; do not use.
Fourth Six: a jar of wine, two bowls, using earthenware. Present simple offerings
through the window; finally no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: the abyss is not full; already brought level. No blame attaches.
Top Six: bound with cords and ropes, placed among thorns. For three years not
obtained; misfortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, The Repeated Abyss may be read as a pattern of action rather
than a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral mea-
sure govern success or danger.
Repeated Abyss: there is trust; the heart alone succeeds. Action has honor.
Initial Six: repeated abyss, entering the pit within the pit; misfortune.
Second Nine: the abyss has danger; seeking small gains.
Third Six: coming and going through abyss upon abyss, perilous and blocked. En-
tering the pit within the pit; do not use.
Fourth Six: a jar of wine, two bowls, using earthenware. Present simple offerings
through the window; finally no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: the abyss is not full; already brought level. no blame attaches.
Top Six: bound with cords and ropes, placed among thorns. For three years not
obtained; misfortune.

第30 卦
䷝ 离 (Li)
Radiance
原文
离，利贞，亨，畜牝牛吉。
初九，履错然，敬之，无咎。
六二，黄离，元吉。
九三，日昃之离，不鼓缶而歌，则大耊之嗟，凶。
九四，突如其来如，焚如，死如，弃如。
六五，出涕沱若，戚嗟若，吉。
上九，王用出征，有嘉折首，获匪其丑，无咎。
关键词释义
卦名 离（Li） ：丽也，附着而明；明须有所依，柔中而正。
英译标题 Radiance。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
离 丽也，附着而明。
牝牛 柔顺中正而能久养。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
103

104 第30 卦
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Radiance: favorable to maintain constancy; through-going. Keeping a cow is good
fortune.
Initial Nine: steps are crossed and confused; respect them, no blame attaches.
Second Six: yellow radiance; greatly good fortune.
Third Nine: radiance of the setting sun; if not beating the jar and singing, then
sighing over great old age; misfortune.
Fourth Nine: sudden in its coming, burning, dying, abandoned.
Fifth Six: tears stream forth, sorrow and sighing; good fortune.
Top Nine: the king uses this to go campaigning; there is excellence in cutting off the
chief, capturing not the common followers; no blame attaches.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Radiance may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.
Radiance: favorable to maintain constancy; through-going. Keeping a cow is good
fortune.
Initial Nine: steps are crossed and confused; respect them, no blame attaches.
Second Six: yellow radiance; greatly good fortune.
Third Nine: radiance of the setting sun; if not beating the jar and singing, then
sighing over great old age; misfortune.
Fourth Nine: sudden in its coming, burning, dying, abandoned.
Fifth Six: tears stream forth, sorrow and sighing; good fortune.
Top Nine: the king uses this to go campaigning; there is excellence in cutting off the
chief, capturing not the common followers; no blame attaches.

本卦义例。“离”有附着与明丽双义，Radiance 只是可读标题，注中保留 dependence。

言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第31 卦
䷞ 咸 (Xian)
Mutual Influence
原文
咸，亨利贞，取女吉。
初六，咸其拇。
六二，咸其腓，凶，居吉。
九三，咸其股，执其随，往吝。
九四，贞吉，悔亡。憧憧往来，朋从尔思。
九五，咸其脢，无悔。
上六，咸其辅颊舌。
关键词释义
卦名 咸（Xian） ：感应相与；情动而贵正，通乎婚姻与人伦。
英译标题 Mutual Influence。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留
专名身份。
咸 感也；互相感应。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
106

107
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Influence: through-going and favorablely steadfast. Taking a woman is good for-
tune.
Initial Six: influence in the big toe.
Second Six: influence in the calf; misfortune. Staying still is good fortune.
Third Nine: influence in the thigh; holding to what follows; to go brings regret.
Fourth Nine: constancy brings good fortune; regret vanishes. Restless coming and
going; friends follow your thoughts.
Fifth Nine: influence in the back; no regret.
Top Six: influence in the jaws, cheeks, and tongue.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Mutual Influence may be read as a pattern of action rather than
a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Influence: through-going and favorablely steadfast. Taking a woman is good for-
tune.
Initial Six: influence in the big toe.
Second Six: influence in the calf; misfortune. Staying still is good fortune.
Third Nine: influence in the thigh; holding to what follows; to go brings regret.
Fourth Nine: constancy brings good fortune; regret vanishes. Restless coming and
going; friends follow your thoughts.
Fifth Nine: influence in the back; no regret.
Top Six: influence in the jaws, cheeks, and tongue.

为 misfortune，指行为与时位相违所趋向的败坏或危险。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第32 卦
䷟ 恒 (Heng)
Duration
原文
恒，亨，无咎，利贞，利有攸往。
初六，浚恒，贞凶，无攸利。
九二，悔亡。
九三，不恒其德，或承之羞，贞吝。
九四，田无禽。
六五，恒其德贞，妇人吉，夫子凶。
上六，振恒，凶。
关键词释义
卦名 恒（Heng） ：久而能常；常中有变，变中守德。
英译标题 Duration。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
恒 常久；非僵固，而是在变中守常。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
贞凶 虽持守而所守失时或失位，故成凶。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
109

110 第32 卦
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Duration: through-going; no blame attaches. Favorable to be steadfast; favorable
to set out.
Initial Six: digging too deeply for duration; constancy misfortune, nothing is favor-
able.
Second Nine: regret vanishes.
Third Nine: not enduring in virtue; perhaps bearing shame; constancy brings re-
gret.
Fourth Nine: hunting, no game.
Fifth Six: enduring in virtuous constancy; good fortune for a woman, misfortune
for the master.
Top Six: shaking duration; misfortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Duration may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.
Duration: through-going; no blame attaches. Favorable to be steadfast; favorable
to set out.
Initial Six: digging too deeply for duration; constancy misfortune, nothing is favor-
able.
Second Nine: regret vanishes.
Third Nine: not enduring in virtue; perhaps bearing shame; constancy brings re-
gret.
Fourth Nine: hunting, no game.

111
Fifth Six: enduring in virtuous constancy; good fortune for a woman, misfortune
for the master.
Top Six: shaking duration; misfortune.
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Duration: through-going; no blame attaches. Favorable to be steadfast; favorable
to set out.
Initial Six: digging too deeply for duration; constancy misfortune, nothing is favor-
able.
Second Nine: regret vanishes.
Third Nine: not enduring in virtue; perhaps bearing shame; constancy brings re-
gret.
Fourth Nine: hunting, no game.
Fifth Six: enduring in virtuous constancy; good fortune for a woman, misfortune
for the master.
Top Six: shaking duration; misfortune.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Heng is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Duration,
is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the original term.
The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the Great
Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an English
reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across all sixty-
four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divination
or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排
印， 标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。 卦名保留拼音Heng， 英文标题 “Duration”
只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“恒”不是僵固不变，而是在变中守常。
术语取舍。“利贞” 译为favorable through constancy， 不译成profitable divination。 “无
咎”统一为 no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “往”译为go / set out，
说明其可否取决于时位，不等于一般行动自由。 “悔”译为regret，取可反省、可转圜之悔，
不作最终灾祸。 “吝”译为regret / shame / distress according to context，重在窘迫与

112 第32 卦
可羞之迹。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随机好运。 “凶”译
为 misfortune，指行为与时位相违所趋向的败坏或危险。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第33 卦
䷠ 遁 (Dun)
Retreat
原文
遁亨，小利贞。
初六，遁尾厉，勿用有攸往。
六二，执之用黄牛之革，莫之胜说。
九三，系遁，有疾厉，畜臣妾吉。
九四，好遁，君子吉，小人否。
九五，嘉遁，贞吉。
上九，肥遁，无不利。
关键词释义
卦名 遁（Dun） ：时不可为而退；退以全其正。
英译标题 Retreat。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
遁 退避；退不是怯，而是全正。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
小人 德量狭小、不能承担公义者；不仅指社会地位卑微者。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
113

114 第33 卦
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Retreat: through-going; small things are favorable through constancy.
Initial Six: retreating at the tail is perilous; do not set out anywhere.
Second Six: holding fast with yellow oxhide; none can loosen it.
Third Nine: tied retreat; illness and peril. Keeping servants is good fortune.
Fourth Nine: good retreat; good fortune for the noble one, not for the small person.
Fifth Nine: excellent retreat; constancy brings good fortune.
Top Nine: ample retreat; nothing unfavorable.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Retreat may be read as a pattern of action rather than a detached
prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure govern suc-
cess or danger.
Retreat: through-going; small things are favorable through constancy.
Initial Six: retreating at the tail is perilous; do not set out anywhere.
Second Six: holding fast with yellow oxhide; none can loosen it.
Third Nine: tied retreat; illness and peril. Keeping servants is good fortune.
Fourth Nine: good retreat; good fortune for the noble one, not for the small person.
Fifth Nine: excellent retreat; constancy brings good fortune.
Top Nine: ample retreat; nothing unfavorable.
最终推荐的深度文化译文

Initial Six: retreating at the tail is perilous; do not set out anywhere.
Second Six: holding fast with yellow oxhide; none can loosen it.
Third Nine: tied retreat; illness and peril. Keeping servants is good fortune.
Fourth Nine: good retreat; good fortune for the noble one, not for the small person.

本卦义例。本卦底本卦名作“遁” ，本简体终校作“遁” ；退避不是怯懦，而是守正全身。

第34 卦
䷡ 大壮 (Da Zhuang)
Great Strength
原文
大壮，利贞。
初九，壮于趾，征凶，有孚。
九二，贞吉。
九三，小人用壮，君子用罔，贞厉。羝羊触藩，羸其角。
九四，贞吉，悔亡。藩决不羸，壮于大舆之輹。
六五，丧羊于易，无悔。
上六，羝羊触藩，不能退，不能遂。无攸利，艰则吉。
关键词释义
卦名 大壮（Da Zhuang） ：壮大之时须正；不可恃强妄动。
英译标题 Great Strength。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名
身份。
大壮 阳盛壮大；壮而须正。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
小人 德量狭小、不能承担公义者；不仅指社会地位卑微者。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
116

117
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Great Strength: favorable to maintain constancy.
Initial Nine: strength in the toes; to campaign is misfortune. There is trust.
Second Nine: constancy brings good fortune.
Third Nine: the small person uses strength; the noble one uses restraint. Constancy
is perilous. A ram butts the hedge and entangles its horns.
Fourth Nine: constancy brings good fortune; regret vanishes. The hedge opens, no
entanglement; strength is in the great wagon’s axle strap.
Fifth Six: losing the sheep in an open place; no regret.
Top Six: the ram butts the hedge, unable to retreat or advance. Nothing is favorable;
in hardship, good fortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Great Strength may be read as a pattern of action rather than
a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Great Strength: favorable to maintain constancy.
Initial Nine: strength in the toes; to campaign is misfortune. There is trust.
Second Nine: constancy brings good fortune.
Third Nine: the small person uses strength; the noble one uses restraint. Constancy

Fourth Nine: constancy brings good fortune; regret vanishes. The hedge opens, no
entanglement; strength is in the great wagon’s axle strap.
Fifth Six: losing the sheep in an open place; no regret.

Top Six: the ram butts the hedge, unable to retreat or advance. Nothing is favorable;
in hardship, good fortune.

第35 卦
䷢ 晋 (Jin)
Advancing
原文
晋，康侯用锡马蕃庶，昼日三接。
初六，晋如摧如，贞吉。罔孚，裕无咎。
六二，晋如愁如，贞吉。受兹介福，于其王母。
六三，众允，悔亡。
九四，晋如鼫鼠，贞厉。
六五，悔亡，失得勿恤。往吉，无不利。
上九，晋其角，维用伐邑。厉吉无咎，贞吝。
关键词释义
卦名 晋（Jin） ：明出地上；进升受宠，贵在不失其正。
英译标题 Advancing。 标题取意译， 以便英语读者先得卦象主旨； 拼音保留专名身份。
晋 进也；明出地上而进升。
康侯 受宠任事之侯。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
侯 侯伯之位；多指新秩序建立时的分封、任命与组织化。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
120

121
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Advancing: the Kang-hou is granted many horses; in one day received three times.
Initial Six: advancing as if pushed back; constancy brings good fortune. Lacking
trust, be generous: no blame attaches.
Second Six: advancing in sorrow; constancy brings good fortune. Receiving this
great blessing from the royal mother.
Third Six: the many consent; regret vanishes.
Fourth Nine: advancing like a greedy rat; constancy perilous.
Fifth Six: regret vanishes; do not worry over loss or gain. To go is good fortune,
nothing unfavorable.
Top Nine: advancing with the horns; use only to attack one’s own town. Perilous
but good fortune, no blame; constancy brings regret.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Advancing may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.
Advancing: the Kang-hou is granted many horses; in one day received three times.
Initial Six: advancing as if pushed back; constancy brings good fortune. Lacking
trust, be generous: no blame attaches.
Second Six: advancing in sorrow; constancy brings good fortune. Receiving this
great blessing from the royal mother.
Third Six: the many consent; regret vanishes.
Fourth Nine: advancing like a greedy rat; constancy perilous.
Fifth Six: regret vanishes; do not worry over loss or gain. To go is good fortune,
nothing unfavorable.

122 第35 卦
Top Nine: advancing with the horns; use only to attack one’s own town. Perilous
but good fortune, no blame attaches; constancy brings regret.
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Advancing: the Kang-hou is granted many horses; in one day received three times.
Initial Six: advancing as if pushed back; constancy brings good fortune. Lacking
trust, be generous: no blame attaches.
Second Six: advancing in sorrow; constancy brings good fortune. Receiving this
great blessing from the royal mother.
Third Six: the many consent; regret vanishes.
Fourth Nine: advancing like a greedy rat; constancy perilous.
Fifth Six: regret vanishes; do not worry over loss or gain. To go is good fortune,
nothing unfavorable.
Top Nine: advancing with the horns; use only to attack one’s own town. Perilous
but good fortune, no blame attaches; constancy brings regret.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Jin is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Advancing,
is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the original term.
The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the Great
Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an English
reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across all sixty-
four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divination
or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排
印， 标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。 卦名保留拼音Jin， 英文标题 “Advancing”
只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“晋”译为 Advance，说明其为明出地上、受命而进。
术语取舍。“贞吉”译作constancy brings good fortune，强调吉由守正而来。 “无咎”统
一为 no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “往”译为go / set out，说明
其可否取决于时位，不等于一般行动自由。 “悔”译为regret，取可反省、可转圜之悔，不
作最终灾祸。 “吝”译为regret / shame / distress according to context，重在窘迫与可
羞之迹。 “厉”译为peril，不等同于 misfortune；它提示戒惧而非判定终局。 “吉”译为

123
good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随机好运。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第36 卦
䷣ 明夷 (Ming Yi)
Darkening of the Light
原文
明夷，利艰贞。
初九，明夷于飞，垂其翼，君子于行，三日不食。有攸往，主人有言。
六二，明夷，夷于左股，用拯马壮吉。
九三，明夷于南狩，得其大首，不可疾贞。
六四，入于左腹，获明夷之心，于出门庭。
六五，箕子之明夷，利贞。
上六，不明晦，初登于天，后入于地。
关键词释义
卦名 明夷（Ming Yi） ：明入地中；光明受伤，君子韬光守艰贞。
英译标题 Darkening of the Light。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音
保留专名身份。
明夷 光明受伤；韬光守艰贞。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
124

125
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Darkening of the Light: favorable in difficult constancy.
Initial Nine: light darkened in flight, drooping its wing. The noble one travels, not
eating for three days. Having somewhere to go, the host has words.
Second Six: light darkened, injured in the left thigh; use a strong horse to rescue:
good fortune.
Third Nine: light darkened in southern hunting; gaining the great chief. Do not be
hasty in constancy.
Fourth Six: entering the left belly, gaining the heart of darkened light; going out
through gate and court.
Fifth Six: the darkening of Jizi; favorable to maintain constancy.
Top Six: not bright but dark; first rising to heaven, afterward entering the earth.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Darkening of the Light may be read as a pattern of action rather
than a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral mea-
sure govern success or danger.
Darkening of the Light: favorable in difficult constancy.
Initial Nine: light darkened in flight, drooping its wing. The noble one travels, not
eating for three days. Having somewhere to go, the host has words.
Second Six: light darkened, injured in the left thigh; use a strong horse to rescue:
good fortune.
Third Nine: light darkened in southern hunting; gaining the great chief. Do not be
hasty in constancy.
Fourth Six: entering the left belly, gaining the heart of darkened light; going out
through gate and court.
Fifth Six: the darkening of Jizi; favorable to maintain constancy.
Top Six: not bright but dark; first rising to heaven, afterward entering the earth.

English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Ming Yi is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Dark-
ening of the Light, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for
the original term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble
one, the Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so
that an English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes
across all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical
divination or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image,
timing, position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、卦名、卦辞、爻位与爻辞逐项校入；本终校本采用简
体排印，标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。卦名保留拼音 Ming Yi，英文标题
“Darkening of the Light”只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“明夷”译为 Darkening of the Light，保留光明受伤而守艰贞。
术语取舍。“利贞” 译为favorable through constancy， 不译成profitable divination。 “往”
译为go / set out， 说明其可否取决于时位， 不等于一般行动自由。 “吉”译为good fortune，

免 gentleman 的阶级和社交色彩。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。

言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第37 卦
䷤ 家人 (Jia Ren)
The Family
原文
家人，利女贞。
初九，闲有家，悔亡。
六二，无攸遂，在中馈，贞吉。
九三，家人嗃嗃，悔厉吉。妇子嘻嘻，终吝。
六四，富家，大吉。
九五，王假有家，勿恤，吉。
上九，有孚威如，终吉。
关键词释义
卦名 家人（Jia Ren） ：家道之正；以内治为天下秩序之本。
英译标题 The Family。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身
份。
家人 家道；内正而外治可推。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
127

128 第37 卦
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
The Family: favorable for the woman’s constancy.
Initial Nine: guarding the household; regret vanishes.
Second Six: no pursuit of her own; in the inner household, providing food; con-
stancy brings good fortune.
Third Nine: household members are stern; regret and peril, yet good fortune. Wife
and children laugh; in the end regret.
Fourth Six: enriching the household; greatly good fortune.
Fifth Nine: the king comes to possess a household; do not worry, good fortune.
Top Nine: there is trust and dignity; finally good fortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, The Family may be read as a pattern of action rather than a
detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
The Family: favorable for the woman’s constancy.
Initial Nine: guarding the household; regret vanishes.
Second Six: no pursuit of her own; in the inner household, providing food; con-
stancy brings good fortune.
Third Nine: household members are stern; regret and peril, yet good fortune. Wife
and children laugh; in the end regret.
Fourth Six: enriching the household; greatly good fortune.
Fifth Nine: the king comes to possess a household; do not worry, good fortune.
Top Nine: there is trust and dignity; finally good fortune.
最终推荐的深度文化译文

Initial Nine: guarding the household; regret vanishes.

第38 卦
䷥ 睽 (Kui)
Divergence
原文
睽，小事吉。
初九，悔亡，丧马勿逐自复。见恶人，无咎。
九二，遇主于巷，无咎。
六三，见舆曳，其牛掣。其人天且劓，无初有终。
九四，睽孤，遇元夫。交孚，厉，无咎。
六五，悔亡。厥宗噬肤，往何咎？
上九，睽孤，见豕负涂，载鬼一车。先张之弧，后说之弧。匪寇婚媾。往，遇雨则吉。
关键词释义
卦名 睽（Kui） ：乖离相违；小事可成，大同未至。
英译标题 Divergence。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身
份。
睽 乖离；异中有通，小事可吉。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
130

131
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Divergence: small affairs are good fortune.
Initial Nine: regret vanishes. Losing a horse, do not pursue; it returns by itself.
Seeing bad people, no blame attaches.
Second Nine: meeting the lord in an alley; no blame attaches.
Third Six: seeing the wagon dragged and the oxen checked; the person is branded
and nose-cut. No beginning, but an end.
Fourth Nine: isolated in divergence, meeting the prime man. Mutual trust; peril, no
blame attaches.
Fifth Six: regret vanishes. His kin bite through the flesh; going, what blame?
Top Nine: isolated in divergence, seeing a pig covered with mud and a cart full of
ghosts. First he draws the bow, later releases it. Not robbers, but marriage allies.
Go; meeting rain is good fortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Divergence may be read as a pattern of action rather than a
detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Divergence: small affairs are good fortune.
Initial Nine: regret vanishes. Losing a horse, do not pursue; it returns by itself.
Seeing bad people, no blame attaches.
Second Nine: meeting the lord in an alley; no blame attaches.
Third Six: seeing the wagon dragged and the oxen checked; the person is branded
and nose-cut. No beginning, but an end.
Fourth Nine: isolated in divergence, meeting the prime man. Mutual trust; peril, no
blame attaches.
Fifth Six: regret vanishes. His kin bite through the flesh; going, what blame?
Top Nine: isolated in divergence, seeing a pig covered with mud and a cart full of
ghosts. First he draws the bow, later releases it. Not robbers, but marriage allies.
Go; meeting rain is good fortune.

第39 卦
䷦ 蹇 (Jian)
Obstruction
原文
蹇，利西南，不利东北。利见大人，贞吉。
初六，往蹇来誉。
六二，王臣蹇蹇，匪躬之故。
九三，往蹇来反。
六四，往蹇来连。
九五，大蹇朋来。
上六，往蹇来硕，吉，利见大人。
关键词释义
卦名 蹇（Jian） ：前行艰阻；宜反身求助，利西南而利见大人。
英译标题 Obstruction。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身
份。
蹇 艰阻；宜反身求助。
西南/东北 以方位象示利害所向。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
利见大人 宜亲近、咨取或得见德位相称者，以定方向。
大人 德位相称、能定大局者；英译作 the Great Person。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
134

135
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Obstruction: favorable in the southwest, not favorable in the northeast. Favorable
to see the Great Person; constancy brings good fortune.
Initial Six: going brings obstruction, coming brings praise.
Second Six: the king’s servant struggles through obstruction, not for his own body’
s sake.
Third Nine: going brings obstruction, coming brings return.
Fourth Six: going brings obstruction, coming brings connection.
Fifth Nine: great obstruction; friends come.
Top Six: going brings obstruction, coming brings greatness; good fortune. Favorable
to see the Great Person.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Obstruction may be read as a pattern of action rather than a
detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Obstruction: favorable in the southwest, not favorable in the northeast. Favorable
to see the Great Person; constancy brings good fortune.
Initial Six: going brings obstruction, coming brings praise.
Second Six: the king’s servant struggles through obstruction, not for his own body’
s sake.
Third Nine: going brings obstruction, coming brings return.
Fourth Six: going brings obstruction, coming brings connection.
Fifth Nine: great obstruction; friends come.
Top Six: going brings obstruction, coming brings greatness; good fortune. Favorable
to see the Great Person.

136 第39 卦
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Obstruction: favorable in the southwest, not favorable in the northeast. Favorable
to see the Great Person; constancy brings good fortune.
Initial Six: going brings obstruction, coming brings praise.
Second Six: the king’s servant struggles through obstruction, not for his own body’
s sake.
Third Nine: going brings obstruction, coming brings return.
Fourth Six: going brings obstruction, coming brings connection.
Fifth Nine: great obstruction; friends come.
Top Six: going brings obstruction, coming brings greatness; good fortune. Favorable
to see the Great Person.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Jian is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Obstruc-
tion, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the original
term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the
Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an
English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across
all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divina-
tion or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排印，
标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。 卦名保留拼音Jian， 英文标题 “Obstruction”
只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“蹇”按艰阻、反身与求助处理；方位象保留不强释。
术语取舍。“贞吉”译作constancy brings good fortune， 强调吉由守正而来。 “利见大人”
译作favorable to see/behold the Great Person，既保留见贤取法，也保留政治伦理中的
定向作用。 “往”译为go / set out，说明其可否取决于时位，不等于一般行动自由。 “吉”
译为 good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随机好运。 “大人”译为the Great
Person，指德位相称、足以定向共同体者，不是普通重要人物。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第40 卦
䷧ 解 (Jie)
Release
原文
解，利西南。无所往，其来复吉；有攸往，夙吉。
初六，无咎。
九二，田获三狐，得黄矢，贞吉。
六三，负且乘，致寇至，贞吝。
九四，解而拇，朋至斯孚。
六五，君子维有解，吉，有孚于小人。
上六，公用射隼于高墉之上，获之，无不利。
关键词释义
卦名 解（Jie） ：险难既解；宜速去其结，宽简以复常。
英译标题 Release。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
解 解除险难；宜速去其结。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
小人 德量狭小、不能承担公义者；不仅指社会地位卑微者。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
137

138 第40 卦
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Release: favorable in the southwest. If there is nowhere to go, returning is good
fortune; if there is somewhere to go, going early is good fortune.
Initial Six: no blame attaches.
Second Nine: hunting, one catches three foxes and obtains a yellow arrow; con-
stancy brings good fortune.
Third Six: carrying a burden and riding in a carriage; this brings robbers. Con-
stancy brings regret.
Fourth Nine: release your big toe; when friends arrive, trust follows.
Fifth Six: the noble one alone has release; good fortune. There is trust toward small
persons.
Top Six: the duke uses this to shoot a hawk atop the high wall and obtains it; nothing
unfavorable.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Release may be read as a pattern of action rather than a detached
prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure govern suc-
cess or danger.

fortune; if there is somewhere to go, going early is good fortune.
Initial Six: no blame attaches.
Second Nine: hunting, one catches three foxes and obtains a yellow arrow; con-
stancy brings good fortune.
Third Six: carrying a burden and riding in a carriage; this brings robbers. Con-
stancy brings regret.
Fourth Nine: release your big toe; when friends arrive, trust follows.
Fifth Six: the noble one alone has release; good fortune. There is trust toward small
persons.

Top Six: the duke uses this to shoot a hawk atop the high wall and obtains it; nothing
unfavorable.

English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Jie is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Release,
is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the original term.
The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the Great
Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an English
reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across all sixty-
four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divination
or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、卦名、卦辞、爻位与爻辞逐项校入；本终校本采用简体
排印， 标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。 卦名保留拼音Jie， 英文标题 “Release”
只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“解”是解除结滞，译文强调解难之后宜返安。
术语取舍。“贞吉”译作constancy brings good fortune， 强调吉由守正而来。 “无咎”统一
为no blame attaches， 不作 “没有问题” 的泛化说法。 “有孚” 译作there is trust/sincerity，
指内在可信之实，不只是主观相信。 “往”译为go / set out，说明其可否取决于时位，不
等于一般行动自由。 “吝”译为regret / shame / distress according to context，重在窘
迫与可羞之迹。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随机好运。 “君

140 第40 卦
子”译为the noble one，指修德成位者，避免gentleman 的阶级和社交色彩。 “小人”译
为 the small person，指德量狭小者，不简单等同社会身份低者。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化

言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第41 卦
䷨ 损 (Sun)
Decrease
原文
损，有孚，元吉，无咎，可贞，利有攸往。曷之用？二簋可用享。
初九，已事遄往，无咎。酌损之。
九二，利贞，征凶。弗损，益之。
六三，三人行，则损一人；一人行，则得其友。
六四，损其疾，使遄有喜。无咎。
六五，或益之十朋之龟，弗克违，元吉。
上九，弗损，益之。无咎，贞吉，利有攸往。得臣无家。
关键词释义
卦名 损（Sun） ：减损非败；损欲益德，损下亦须有孚。
英译标题 Decrease。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
损 减损；损欲益德，非单纯损失。
二簋 薄祭而诚，重诚不重侈。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
141

142 第41 卦
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Decrease: there is trust; greatly good fortune, no blame attaches. One may be stead-
fast; favorable to set out. What to use? Two bowls may be used for offering.
Initial Nine: when affairs are done, go quickly; no blame attaches. Consider how to
decrease it.
Second Nine: favorable to maintain constancy; to set forth brings misfortune. Do
not decrease; increase it.
Third Six: when three people walk, one is decreased; when one walks, he gains a
friend.
Fourth Six: decreasing his illness; making haste brings joy. No blame attaches.
Fifth Six: someone increases him with a turtle worth ten pairs; he cannot refuse.
Greatly good fortune.
Top Nine: do not decrease; increase it. No blame, constancy brings good fortune,
favorable to go somewhere. Gaining servants, no household attachment.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Decrease may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.

decrease it.
Second Nine: favorable to maintain constancy; to set forth brings misfortune. Do
not decrease; increase it.

friend.
Fourth Six: decreasing his illness; making haste brings joy. no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: someone increases him with a turtle worth ten pairs; he cannot refuse.
Greatly good fortune.
Top Nine: do not decrease; increase it. no blame attaches, constancy brings good
fortune, favorable to go somewhere. Gaining servants, no household attachment.

第42 卦
䷩ 益 (Yi)
Increase
原文
益，利有攸往，利涉大川。
初九，利用为大作，元吉，无咎。
六二，或益之十朋之龟，弗克违，永贞吉。王用享于帝，吉。
六三，益之用凶事，无咎。有孚中行，告公用圭。
六四，中行，告公从，利用为依迁国。
九五，有孚惠心，勿问，元吉。有孚惠我德。
上九，莫益之，或击之。立心勿恒，凶。
关键词释义
卦名 益（Yi） ：增益非私利；贵在惠下、大作与涉险成事。
英译标题 Increase。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
益 增益；惠下与大作。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
涉大川 涉险成事；指重大行动与跨越艰难处境。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
145

146 第42 卦
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Increase: favorable to set out; favorable to cross the great river.
Initial Nine: favorable to use for great works; greatly good fortune, no blame at-
taches.
Second Six: someone increases him with a turtle worth ten pairs; he cannot refuse.
Enduring constancy brings good fortune. The king uses this to offer to the Lord on
High; good fortune.
Third Six: increasing him through misfortune affairs; no blame attaches. With trust
and middle conduct, report to the duke using a jade tablet.
Fourth Six: middle conduct; report to the duke and he follows. Favorable to use as
support in moving the state.
Fifth Nine: there is trust and a beneficent heart; do not ask. Greatly good fortune.
Trust benefits my virtue.
Top Nine: none increases him; someone strikes him. Setting the heart without con-
stancy: misfortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Increase may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.

Initial Nine: favorable to use for great works; greatly good fortune, no blame at-
taches.
Second Six: someone increases him with a turtle worth ten pairs; he cannot refuse.
Enduring constancy brings good fortune. The king uses this to offer to the Lord on
High; good fortune.

147
Third Six: increasing him through misfortune affairs; no blame attaches. With trust
and middle conduct, report to the duke using a jade tablet.
Fourth Six: middle conduct; report to the duke and he follows. Favorable to use as
support in moving the state.
Fifth Nine: there is trust and a beneficent heart; do not ask. Greatly good fortune.
Trust benefits my virtue.
Top Nine: none increases him; someone strikes him. Setting the heart without con-
stancy: misfortune.

Fourth Six: middle conduct; report to the duke and he follows. Favorable to use as
support in moving the state.
Fifth Nine: there is trust and a beneficent heart; do not ask. Greatly good fortune.
Trust benefits my virtue.
Top Nine: none increases him; someone strikes him. Setting the heart without con-
stancy: misfortune.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Yi is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Increase,
is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the original term.
The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the Great
Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an English
reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across all sixty-
four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divination
or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.

148 第42 卦
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排
印，标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。卦名保留拼音Yi，英文标题“Increase”
只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“益”不作个人获利，而作增益、惠下与大作。
术语取舍。“贞吉”译作constancy brings good fortune， 强调吉由守正而来。 “无咎”统一
为no blame attaches， 不作 “没有问题” 的泛化说法。 “有孚” 译作there is trust/sincerity，
指内在可信之实，不只是主观相信。 “涉大川”保留cross the great river的古典象，不改
写成undertake a big project，但在注释中说明为涉险任大事。 “往”译为go / set out，说
明其可否取决于时位，不等于一般行动自由。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境
判断，不等于随机好运。 “凶”译为misfortune，指行为与时位相违所趋向的败坏或危险。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第43 卦
䷪ 夬 (Guai)
Resolution
原文
夬，扬于王庭，孚号有厉。告自邑，不利即戎，利有攸往。
初九，壮于前趾，往不胜为咎。
九二，惕号，莫夜有戎，勿恤。
九三，壮于頄，有凶。君子夬夬，独行遇雨，若濡有愠，无咎。
九四，臀无肤，其行次且。牵羊悔亡，闻言不信。
九五，苋陆夬夬，中行无咎。
上六，无号，终有凶。
关键词释义
卦名 夬（Guai） ：决去阴邪；宜宣告而不宜好战。
英译标题 Resolution。 标题取意译， 以便英语读者先得卦象主旨； 拼音保留专名身份。
夬 决也；决去阴邪而戒用武。
王庭 公庭之上，须明告而正名。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
149

150 第43 卦
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Resolution: declared in the royal court; truthful cry, with danger. Announce from
one’s own town. Not favorable to take up arms; favorable to set out.
Initial Nine: strength in the front toes; going without victory is blame.
Second Nine: alarmed cry; at night there are arms. Do not worry.
Third Nine: strength in the cheekbones; there is misfortune. The noble one resolves
resolutely; walking alone, meeting rain, wet and annoyed, no blame attaches.
Fourth Nine: the buttocks have no skin; walking is halting. Lead the sheep and
regret vanishes; hearing words, he does not believe.
Fifth Nine: amaranth on high ground, resolutely cut; middle conduct, no blame
attaches.
Top Six: no cry; in the end there is misfortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Resolution may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.
Resolution: declared in the royal court; truthful cry, with danger. Announce from
one’s own town. Not favorable to take up arms; favorable to set out.
Initial Nine: strength in the front toes; going without victory is blame.
Second Nine: alarmed cry; at night there are arms. Do not worry.
Third Nine: strength in the cheekbones; there is misfortune. The noble one resolves
resolutely; walking alone, meeting rain, wet and annoyed, no blame attaches.
Fourth Nine: the buttocks have no skin; walking is halting. Lead the sheep and
regret vanishes; hearing words, he does not believe.
Fifth Nine: amaranth on high ground, resolutely cut; middle conduct, no blame
attaches.
Top Six: no cry; in the end there is misfortune.

one’s own town. Not favorable to take up arms; favorable to set out.

English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Guai is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Resolu-
tion, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the original
term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the
Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an
English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across
all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divina-
tion or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排印，
标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。 卦名保留拼音Guai， 英文标题“Resolution”
只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“夬”译为 Resolution/Breakthrough，强调决断而戒暴。
术语取舍。“无咎”统一为 no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “往”译
为 go / set out，说明其可否取决于时位，不等于一般行动自由。 “悔”译为regret，取可
反省、可转圜之悔，不作最终灾祸。 “厉”译为peril，不等同于misfortune；它提示戒惧
而非判定终局。 “凶”译为misfortune，指行为与时位相违所趋向的败坏或危险。 “君子”
译为 the noble one，指修德成位者，避免 gentleman 的阶级和社交色彩。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。

第44 卦
䷫ 姤 (Gou)
Encounter
原文
姤，女壮，勿用取女。
初六，系于金柅，贞吉。有攸往，见凶。羸豕孚蹢躅。
九二，包有鱼，无咎，不利宾。
九三，臀无肤，其行次且。厉，无大咎。
九四，包无鱼，起凶。
九五，以杞包瓜，含章，有陨自天。
上九，姤其角，吝，无咎。
关键词释义
卦名 姤（Gou） ：不期而遇；阴长初萌，须防微杜渐。
英译标题 Encounter。 标题取意译， 以便英语读者先得卦象主旨； 拼音保留专名身份。
姤 遇也；不期而遇。
女壮 阴长之初，须防势盛。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
153

154 第44 卦
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Encounter: the woman is strong; do not take the woman.
Initial Six: tied to a metal brake; constancy brings good fortune. Having somewhere
to go, one sees misfortune. The lean pig truly struggles.
Second Nine: a bundle containing fish; no blame attaches. Not favorable for guests.
Third Nine: buttocks with no skin; walking halting. Perilous, no great blame.
Fourth Nine: the bundle has no fish; rising brings misfortune.
Fifth Nine: using willow to wrap the melon; holding brilliance within, something
falls from Heaven.
Top Nine: encountering with the horns; regret, no blame attaches.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Encounter may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.

falls from Heaven.
Top Nine: encountering with the horns; regret, no blame attaches.

第45 卦
䷬ 萃 (Cui)
Gathering
原文
萃，亨。王假有庙，利见大人。亨利贞，用大牲吉，利有攸往。
初六，有孚不终，乃乱乃萃。若号，一握为笑，勿恤，往无咎。
六二，引吉无咎，孚乃利用禴。
六三，萃如嗟如，无攸利。往无咎，小吝。
九四，大吉无咎。
九五，萃有位，无咎。匪孚，元永贞，悔亡。
上六，赍咨涕洟，无咎。
关键词释义
卦名 萃（Cui） ：聚合众人；以宗庙礼义凝聚共同体。
英译标题 Gathering。标题取意译， 以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
萃 聚也；群体凝聚须以礼义。
庙 宗庙，象共同记忆与秩序。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
利见大人 宜亲近、咨取或得见德位相称者，以定方向。
有攸往 有所前往、有所施行；常关联时机是否成熟。
大人 德位相称、能定大局者；英译作 the Great Person。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
156

157
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Gathering: through-going. The king comes to the ancestral temple; favorable to see
the Great Person. Through-going and favorablely steadfast. Using great victims is
good fortune; favorable to set out.
Initial Six: there is trust but not to the end; then disorder, then gathering. If calling
out, one grasp becomes laughter. Do not worry; to go, no blame attaches.
Second Six: being drawn forward is good fortune, no blame attaches. With trust,
the simple offering is favorable.
Third Six: gathering and sighing; nothing is favorable. To go, no blame, small regret.
Fourth Nine: greatly good fortune, no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: gathering with position; no blame attaches. If not yet trusted, originary
enduring constancy makes regret vanish.
Top Six: lamenting, tears and sniveling; no blame attaches.
面向英语母语者的自然意译

tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.
Gathering: through-going. The king comes to the ancestral temple; favorable to see
the Great Person. Through-going and favorablely steadfast. Using great victims is
good fortune; favorable to set out.

Second Six: being drawn forward is good fortune, no blame attaches. With trust,
the simple offering is favorable.
Third Six: gathering and sighing; nothing is favorable. To go, no blame attaches,
small regret.
Fourth Nine: greatly good fortune, no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: gathering with position; no blame attaches. If not yet trusted, originary
enduring constancy makes regret vanish.
Top Six: lamenting, tears and sniveling; no blame attaches.

中文翻译取舍说明

咎” 统一为no blame attaches， 不作 “没有问题” 的泛化说法。 “有孚” 译作there is trust/s-

在窘迫与可羞之迹。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随机好运。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第46 卦
䷭ 升 (Sheng)
Ascending
原文
升，元亨。用见大人，勿恤，南征吉。
初六，允升，大吉。
九二，孚乃利用禴，无咎。
九三，升虚邑。
六四，王用亨于岐山，吉，无咎。
六五，贞吉，升阶。
上六，冥升，利于不息之贞。
关键词释义
卦名 升（Sheng） ：柔顺上升；积小成高，循序而进。
英译标题 Ascending。 标题取意译， 以便英语读者先得卦象主旨； 拼音保留专名身份。
升 上升；柔顺而渐进。
元亨 元而能通，表示大端已具而其道可行。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
大人 德位相称、能定大局者；英译作 the Great Person。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
160

161
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Ascending: originary and through-going. Use this to see the Great Person; do not
worry. Southward campaign is good fortune.
Initial Six: sincerely ascending; greatly good fortune.
Second Nine: with trust, the simple offering is favorable; no blame attaches.
Third Nine: ascending into an empty city.
Fourth Six: the king uses this to offer at Mount Qi; good fortune, no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: constancy brings good fortune; ascending the steps.
Top Six: dark ascending; favorable for unceasing constancy.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Ascending may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.
Ascending: primal and through-going. Use this to see the Great Person; do not worry.
Southward campaign is good fortune.
Initial Six: sincerely ascending; greatly good fortune.
Second Nine: with trust, the simple offering is favorable; no blame attaches.
Third Nine: ascending into an empty city.
Fourth Six: the king uses this to offer at Mount Qi; good fortune, no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: constancy brings good fortune; ascending the steps.
Top Six: dark ascending; favorable for unceasing constancy.
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Ascending: primal and through-going. Use this to see the Great Person; do not worry.
Southward campaign is good fortune.
Initial Six: sincerely ascending; greatly good fortune.

162 第46 卦
Second Nine: with trust, the simple offering is favorable; no blame attaches.
Third Nine: ascending into an empty city.
Fourth Six: the king uses this to offer at Mount Qi; good fortune, no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: constancy brings good fortune; ascending the steps.
Top Six: dark ascending; favorable for unceasing constancy.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Sheng is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Ascend-
ing, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the original
term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the
Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an
English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across
all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divina-
tion or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排印，
标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。 卦名保留拼音Sheng， 英文标题 “Ascending”
只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“升”是柔顺渐进，不是骤然跃升。
术语取舍。“元亨” 译作primal/originary and through-going， 保留 “大端可通” 之义。 “贞
吉”译作constancy brings good fortune，强调吉由守正而来。 “无咎”统一为no blame
attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “征”按主动推进、出行或征伐译出，随卦爻语
境在set forth / campaign / go forth间取舍。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处
境判断，不等于随机好运。 “大人”译为the Great Person，指德位相称、足以定向共同体
者，不是普通重要人物。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第47 卦
䷮ 困 (Kun)
Oppression
原文
困，亨，贞大人吉，无咎。有言不信。
初六，臀困于株木，入于幽谷，三岁不觌。
九二，困于酒食，朱绂方来，利用享祀，征凶，无咎。
六三，困于石，据于蒺蔾，入于其宫，不见其妻，凶。
九四，来徐徐，困于金车。吝，有终。
九五，劓刖，困于赤绂。乃徐有说，利用祭祀。
上六，困于葛藟，于臲卼，曰动悔有悔，征吉。
关键词释义
卦名 困（Kun） ：困穷之中守德；大人吉而言不见信。
英译标题 Oppression。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身
份。
困 穷困；困而守德。
有言不信 困时言语难取信。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
大人 德位相称、能定大局者；英译作 the Great Person。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
163

164 第47 卦
吝 局促、羞吝、进退失宜；较凶轻而较悔窒。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Oppression: through-going. Constancy of the Great Person is good fortune; no
blame attaches. Words are not believed.
Initial Six: buttocks oppressed by a tree stump; entering a dark valley, for three
years not seen.
Second Nine: oppressed by wine and food; the red knee-covering is coming. Favor-
able to make offering; to set forth brings misfortune, no blame attaches.
Third Six: oppressed by stone, leaning on thorns; entering his palace, not seeing his
wife; misfortune.
Fourth Nine: coming slowly, oppressed by a metal carriage. Regret, yet there is
completion.
Fifth Nine: nose-cut and foot-cut, oppressed by the scarlet knee-covering. Then
slowly there is release; favorable to use sacrifice.
Top Six: oppressed by vines, on uneasy ground. Saying“movement brings regret,”
yet with regret; to campaign is good fortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Oppression may be read as a pattern of action rather than a
detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Oppression: through-going. Constancy of the Great Person is good fortune; no
blame attaches. Words are not believed.
Initial Six: buttocks oppressed by a tree stump; entering a dark valley, for three
years not seen.
Second Nine: oppressed by wine and food; the red knee-covering is coming. Favor-
able to make offering; to set forth brings misfortune, no blame attaches.

slowly there is release; favorable to use sacrifice.
Top Six: oppressed by vines, on uneasy ground. Saying“movement brings regret,”
yet with regret; to campaign is good fortune.

中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排印，

本卦义例。“困”译为 Oppression/Exhaustion，重在困而守德，非纯粹失败。

译为regret，取可反省、可转圜之悔，不作最终灾祸。 “吝”译为regret / shame / distress
according to context，重在窘迫与可羞之迹。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处

言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第48 卦
䷯ 井 (Jing)
The Well
原文
井，改邑不改井，无丧无得，往来井井。汔至，亦未繘井，羸其瓶，凶。
初六，井泥不食，旧井无禽。
九二，井谷射鲋，瓮敝漏。
九三，井渫不食，为我心恻。可用汲，王明并受其福。
六四，井甃无咎。
九五，井洌，寒泉食。
上六，井收勿幕，有孚元吉。
关键词释义
卦名 井（Jing） ：井道不迁；养人而待汲用，功成在及物。
英译标题 The Well。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
井 井道；居其所而养人。
羸其瓶 汲器败坏，功亏于将成。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
王 王者、主政者；在《易》中常兼具政治与礼义责任。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
167

168 第48 卦
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
The Well: changing the town does not change the well. No loss, no gain; going and
coming, welling. Nearly reached, yet the rope has not drawn from the well; the jar
is broken: misfortune.
Initial Six: the well is muddy and not drunk; the old well has no birds.
Second Nine: in the well valley one shoots small fish; the jar is cracked and leaks.
Third Nine: the well is cleaned but not drunk; my heart is sorrowful. It can be
drawn from; if the king is bright, all receive its blessing.
Fourth Six: the well is lined with masonry; no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: the well is clear; the cold spring is drunk.
Top Six: the well is drawn from, do not cover it; with trust, greatly good fortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, The Well may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.

coming, welling. Nearly reached, yet the rope has not drawn from the well; the jar
is broken: misfortune.

Second Nine: in the well valley one shoots small fish; the jar is cracked and leaks.
Third Nine: the well is cleaned but not drunk; my heart is sorrowful. It can be
drawn from; if the king is bright, all receive its blessing.
Fourth Six: the well is lined with masonry; no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: the well is clear; the cold spring is drunk.
Top Six: the well is drawn from, do not cover it; with trust, greatly good fortune.
最终推荐的深度文化译文

coming, welling. Nearly reached, yet the rope has not drawn from the well; the jar
is broken: misfortune.

第49 卦
䷰ 革 (Ge)
Radical Change
原文
革，己日乃孚，元亨利贞，悔亡。
初九，巩用黄牛之革。
六二，己日乃革之，征吉，无咎。
九三，征凶，贞厉。革言三就，有孚。
九四，悔亡，有孚改命吉。
九五，大人虎变，未占有孚。
上六，君子豹变，小人革面。征凶，居贞吉。
关键词释义
卦名 革（Ge） ：变革须有时有信；改命非轻躁，待日乃孚。
英译标题 Radical Change。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专
名身份。
革 变革；须有时、有信、有正。
己日 天干之己日；表示待时而信成。
元亨利贞 四德并举：创始、通达、合宜、正固，构成《易》之基本价值序列。
元亨 元而能通，表示大端已具而其道可行。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
贞吉 守正则吉；吉由行为得正而来。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
有孚 有诚信、有可信之实；不是情绪上的相信。
170

171
君子 修德成位之人；英译作 the noble one，避免阶级化或现代绅士化。
大人 德位相称、能定大局者；英译作 the Great Person。
小人 德量狭小、不能承担公义者；不仅指社会地位卑微者。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Ge: on the ji day, trust is established. Originary, through-going, favorable in con-
stancy; regret vanishes.
Initial Nine: bind firmly with yellow oxhide.
Second Six: on the ji day, change it. To set forth brings good fortune; no blame at-
taches.
Third Nine: to set forth brings misfortune; constancy perilous. Words of change
completed three times: there is trust.
Fourth Nine: regret vanishes; with trust, changing the mandate is good fortune.
Fifth Nine: the Great Person changes like a tiger; before divination there is trust.
Top Six: the noble one changes like a leopard; the small person changes the face. To
set forth brings misfortune; to dwell in constancy brings good fortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Radical Change may be read as a pattern of action rather than
a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure

172 第49 卦
govern success or danger.
Ge: on the ji day, trust is established. Originary, through-going, favorable in con-
stancy; regret vanishes.
Initial Nine: bind firmly with yellow oxhide.
Second Six: on the ji day, change it. To set forth brings good fortune; no blame
attaches.
Third Nine: to set forth brings misfortune; constancy perilous. Words of change
completed three times: there is trust.
Fourth Nine: regret vanishes; with trust, changing the mandate is good fortune.
Fifth Nine: the Great Person changes like a tiger; before divination there is trust.
Top Six: the noble one changes like a leopard; the small person changes the face. To
set forth brings misfortune; to dwell in constancy brings good fortune.
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Ge: on the ji day, trust is established. Originary, through-going, favorable in con-
stancy; regret vanishes.
Initial Nine: bind firmly with yellow oxhide.
Second Six: on the ji day, change it. To set forth brings good fortune; no blame at-
taches.
Third Nine: to set forth brings misfortune; constancy perilous. Words of change
completed three times: there is trust.
Fourth Nine: regret vanishes; with trust, changing the mandate is good fortune.
Fifth Nine: the Great Person changes like a tiger; before divination there is trust.
Top Six: the noble one changes like a leopard; the small person changes the face. To
set forth brings misfortune; to dwell in constancy brings good fortune.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Ge is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Radical
Change, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the origi-
nal term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the
Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an
English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across
all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divina-
tion or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.

173
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、卦名、卦辞、爻位与爻辞逐项校入；本终校本采用简体
排印，标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。卦名保留拼音Ge，英文标题“Radical
Change”只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“己日乃孚”保留天干待时之义；革不是躁进革命，而是有信、有时、有正的改
命。
术语取舍。“元亨利贞”不拆成四个互不相干的吉祥词，而按创始、通达、合宜、正固的义
理序列处理。 “元亨”译作primal/originary and through-going，保留“大端可通”之
义。“利贞”译为favorable through constancy，不译成 profitable divination。“贞
吉”译作constancy brings good fortune，强调吉由守正而来。 “无咎”统一为no blame
attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “有孚”译作there is trust/sincerity，指内在
可信之实，不只是主观相信。 “征”按主动推进、出行或征伐译出，随卦爻语境在set forth
/ campaign / go forth间取舍。 “悔”译为regret，取可反省、可转圜之悔，不作最终灾祸。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第50 卦
䷱ 鼎 (Ding)
The Cauldron
原文
鼎，元吉，亨。
初六，鼎颠趾，利出否，得妾以其子，无咎。
九二，鼎有实，我仇有疾，不我能即，吉。
九三，鼎耳革，其行塞，雉膏不食。方雨亏悔，终吉。
九四，鼎折足，覆公𫗧，其形渥，凶。
六五，鼎黄耳金铉，利贞。
上九，鼎玉铉，大吉，无不利。
关键词释义
卦名 鼎（Ding） ：鼎新与养贤；器成而道成，革故之后以新制养德。
英译标题 The Cauldron。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名
身份。
鼎 器也；鼎新、养贤、成礼之象。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
元 创始、根本、广大；不仅是 great。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
174

175
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Ding: primal good fortune; through-going.
Initial Six: the cauldron overturns its feet; favorable to expel what is bad. Taking a
concubine for her son; no blame attaches.
Second Nine: the cauldron has substance. My opponent has illness and cannot ap-
proach me; good fortune.
Third Nine: the cauldron’s ears are changed; its movement is blocked, pheasant
fat not eaten. When rain comes, regret diminishes; finally good fortune.
Fourth Nine: the cauldron breaks its legs, overturning the duke’s stew; its form is
stained. Misfortune.
Fifth Six: the cauldron has yellow ears and a metal handle; favorable to maintain
constancy.
Top Nine: the cauldron has a jade handle; greatly good fortune, nothing unfavor-
able.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, The Cauldron may be read as a pattern of action rather than
a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Ding: primal good fortune; through-going.
Initial Six: the cauldron overturns its feet; favorable to expel what is bad. Taking a
concubine for her son; no blame attaches.

proach me; good fortune.
Third Nine: the cauldron’s ears are changed; its movement is blocked, pheasant
fat not eaten. When rain comes, regret diminishes; finally good fortune.
Fourth Nine: the cauldron breaks its legs, overturning the duke’s stew; its form is
stained. Misfortune.

176 第50 卦

constancy.

able.

术语取舍。“利贞” 译为favorable through constancy， 不译成profitable divination。 “无

第51 卦
䷲ 震 (Zhen)
Thunder
原文
震亨，震来虩虩，笑言哑哑。震惊百里，不丧匕鬯。
初九，震来虩虩，后笑言哑哑，吉。
六二，震来厉，亿丧贝，跻于九陵。勿逐，七日得。
六三，震苏苏，震行无眚。
九四，震遂泥。
六五，震往来厉，亿无丧有事。
上六，震索索，视矍矍，征凶。震不于其躬，于其邻，无咎。婚媾有言。
关键词释义
卦名 震（Zhen） ：震动惊惧；以恐惧修省而不失祭器。
英译标题 Thunder。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
震 动也、惊也；因惧而修省。
匕鬯 祭器与鬯酒，象敬慎不失其守。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
往 前往、推行；不等于一切行动皆可。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
亨 通达、畅行、可通；英译多作 through-going。
178

179
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Thunder: through-going. Thunder comes, fearfully; then laughter and words.
Thunder shocks a hundred li, yet spoon and sacrificial wine are not lost.
Initial Nine: thunder comes fearfully; afterward laughter and words; good fortune.
Second Six: thunder comes, perilous; losing many cowries, climbing the nine hills.
Do not pursue; in seven days they are regained.
Third Six: thunder leaves one unsettled; moving with the shock, no disaster.
Fourth Nine: thunder sinks into mud.
Fifth Six: thunder going and coming is perilous; though many are not lost, there is
business.
Top Six: thunder leaves one trembling, glancing about; to set forth brings misfor-
tune. If the shock is not on one’s own body but on the neighbor, no blame attaches.
Marriage alliance has words.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Thunder may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.
Thunder: through-going. Thunder comes, fearfully; then laughter and words.
Thunder shocks a hundred li, yet spoon and sacrificial wine are not lost.
Initial Nine: thunder comes fearfully; afterward laughter and words; good fortune.
Second Six: thunder comes, perilous; losing many cowries, climbing the nine hills.
Do not pursue; in seven days they are regained.
Third Six: thunder leaves one unsettled; moving with the shock, no disaster.
Fourth Nine: thunder sinks into mud.
Fifth Six: thunder going and coming is perilous; though many are not lost, there is
business.
Top Six: thunder leaves one trembling, glancing about; to set forth brings misfor-
tune. If the shock is not on one’s own body but on the neighbor, no blame attaches.
Marriage alliance has words.

Thunder: through-going. Thunder comes, fearfully; then laughter and words.
Thunder shocks a hundred li, yet spoon and sacrificial wine are not lost.
Initial Nine: thunder comes fearfully; afterward laughter and words; good fortune.
Second Six: thunder comes, perilous; losing many cowries, climbing the nine hills.
Do not pursue; in seven days they are regained.

English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Zhen is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Thunder,
is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the original term.
The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the Great
Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an English
reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across all sixty-
four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divination
or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排
印， 标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。 卦名保留拼音Zhen， 英文标题 “Thunder”
只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“震”兼雷动与戒惧，译文保留恐惧之后的修省。
术语取舍。“无咎”统一为no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “征”按主
动推进、出行或征伐译出，随卦爻语境在set forth / campaign / go forth间取舍。 “往”译
为 go / set out，说明其可否取决于时位，不等于一般行动自由。 “厉”译为peril，不等同
于 misfortune；它提示戒惧而非判定终局。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境
判断，不等于随机好运。 “凶”译为misfortune，指行为与时位相违所趋向的败坏或危险。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。

第52 卦
䷳ 艮 (Gen)
Stillness
原文
艮其背，不获其身。行其庭，不见其人，无咎。
初六，艮其趾，无咎，利永贞。
六二，艮其腓，不拯其随，其心不快。
九三，艮其限，列其夤，厉薰心。
六四，艮其身，无咎。
六五，艮其辅，言有序，悔亡。
上九，敦艮吉。
关键词释义
卦名 艮（Gen） ：止其所当止；身心各安其位。
英译标题 Stillness。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留专名身份。
艮 止也；止于所当止。
背 不见其身，象止欲与止私。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
悔 过度、失位或失时后的可悔之机；尚含反省转圜。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
182

183
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Still the back, not grasping the body. Walk in the courtyard, not seeing the person.
No blame attaches.
Initial Six: stilling the toes; no blame; favorable in enduring constancy.
Second Six: stilling the calves, not rescuing what follows; the heart is not glad.
Third Nine: stilling the waist, splitting the spine; peril smokes the heart.
Fourth Six: stilling the body; no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: stilling the jaws; speech has order, regret vanishes.
Top Nine: generous stillness; good fortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Stillness may be read as a pattern of action rather than a de-
tached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure gov-
ern success or danger.

no blame attaches.
Initial Six: stilling the toes; no blame attaches; favorable in enduring constancy.
Second Six: stilling the calves, not rescuing what follows; the heart is not glad.
Third Nine: stilling the waist, splitting the spine; peril smokes the heart.
Fourth Six: stilling the body; no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: stilling the jaws; speech has order, regret vanishes.
Top Nine: generous stillness; good fortune.
最终推荐的深度文化译文

no blame attaches.

Second Six: stilling the calves, not rescuing what follows; the heart is not glad.
Third Nine: stilling the waist, splitting the spine; peril smokes the heart.
Fourth Six: stilling the body; no blame attaches.
Fifth Six: stilling the jaws; speech has order, regret vanishes.
Top Nine: generous stillness; good fortune.

术语取舍。“无咎”统一为no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “悔”译为
regret，取可反省、可转圜之悔，不作最终灾祸。 “厉”译为peril，不等同于misfortune；
它提示戒惧而非判定终局。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的处境判断，不等于随
机好运。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第53 卦
䷴ 渐 (Jian)
Gradual Progress
原文
渐，女归吉，利贞。
初六，鸿渐于干，小子厉，有言，无咎。
六二，鸿渐于磐，饮食衎衎，吉。
九三，鸿渐于陆，夫征不复，妇孕不育，凶。利御寇。
六四，鸿渐于木，或得其桷，无咎。
九五，鸿渐于陵，妇三岁不孕。终莫之胜，吉。
上九，鸿渐于陆，其羽可用为仪，吉。
关键词释义
卦名 渐（Jian） ：渐进有序；如鸿之行，婚姻亦贵其序。
英译标题 Gradual Progress。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音保留
专名身份。
渐 渐进；有序而不躁。
鸿 大雁之象，进退有序。
利贞 所利在于守正； “利”不可脱离“贞”而作私利解。
无咎 虽处险境或微有失当，但行为仍得其宜，故无可归咎。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
厉 危厉、危殆；提示须戒惧，不必然等于凶。
185

186 第53 卦
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
Gradual Progress: the woman’s marriage is good fortune; favorable to maintain
constancy.
Initial Six: the wild goose gradually approaches the shore; the young son is in peril,
there are words, no blame attaches.
Second Six: the wild goose gradually approaches the rock; eating and drinking in
ease, good fortune.
Third Nine: the wild goose gradually approaches the plateau; the husband cam-
paigns and does not return, the wife conceives but does not rear. Misfortune. Fa-
vorable to resist robbers.
Fourth Six: the wild goose gradually approaches the tree; perhaps finding a flat
branch. No blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: the wild goose gradually approaches the hill; the woman for three years
does not conceive. In the end none overcomes it; good fortune.
Top Nine: the wild goose gradually approaches the high land; its feathers may be
used for ritual display. Good fortune.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, Gradual Progress may be read as a pattern of action rather than
a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral measure
govern success or danger.
Gradual Progress: the woman’s marriage is good fortune; favorable to maintain
constancy.
Initial Six: the wild goose gradually approaches the shore; the young son is in peril,
there are words, no blame attaches.
Second Six: the wild goose gradually approaches the rock; eating and drinking in
ease, good fortune.
Third Nine: the wild goose gradually approaches the plateau; the husband cam-
paigns and does not return, the wife conceives but does not rear. Misfortune. Fa-

187
vorable to resist robbers.
Fourth Six: the wild goose gradually approaches the tree; perhaps finding a flat
branch. no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: the wild goose gradually approaches the hill; the woman for three years
does not conceive. In the end none overcomes it; good fortune.
Top Nine: the wild goose gradually approaches the high land; its feathers may be
used for ritual display. Good fortune.
最终推荐的深度文化译文
Gradual Progress: the woman’s marriage is good fortune; favorable to maintain
constancy.
Initial Six: the wild goose gradually approaches the shore; the young son is in peril,
there are words, no blame attaches.
Second Six: the wild goose gradually approaches the rock; eating and drinking in
ease, good fortune.
Third Nine: the wild goose gradually approaches the plateau; the husband cam-
paigns and does not return, the wife conceives but does not rear. Misfortune. Fa-
vorable to resist robbers.
Fourth Six: the wild goose gradually approaches the tree; perhaps finding a flat
branch. no blame attaches.
Fifth Nine: the wild goose gradually approaches the hill; the woman for three years
does not conceive. In the end none overcomes it; good fortune.
Top Nine: the wild goose gradually approaches the high land; its feathers may be
used for ritual display. Good fortune.
English philosophical and cultural notes
In this edition, Jian is kept as a technical Chinese name. The English title, Gradual
Progress, is a guide to the image and field of action, not a replacement for the origi-
nal term. The translation therefore keeps a stable vocabulary for the noble one, the
Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so that an
English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes across
all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical divina-
tion or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image, timing,
position, and conduct.

188 第53 卦
中文翻译取舍说明
经文校勘。本卦按所定底本的卦序、 卦名、 卦辞、 爻位与爻辞逐项校入； 本终校本采用简体排
印，标点以现代阅读便利为准而不改变经文字序。卦名保留拼音Jian，英文标题“Gradual
Progress”只作导读性标题，不取代中文卦名。
本卦义例。“渐”以鸿雁有序进退为主象，不译成 general progress。
术语取舍。“利贞” 译为favorable through constancy， 不译成profitable divination。 “无
咎”统一为no blame attaches，不作“没有问题”的泛化说法。 “征”按主动推进、出行
或征伐译出，随卦爻语境在set forth / campaign / go forth间取舍。 “厉”译为peril，不
等同于 misfortune；它提示戒惧而非判定终局。 “吉”译为good fortune，指趋向善成的
处境判断，不等于随机好运。 “凶”译为misfortune，指行为与时位相违所趋向的败坏或
危险。
三层译文关系。“贴近原文的英文直译”尽量保留经文字面顺序和象辞密度； “面向英语母
语者的自然意译”在不增添义理结论的前提下补足英语句法和语境； “最终推荐的深度文化
译文”则在术语稳定、语气庄重和可读性之间取中，适合正文引用。
避免的误读。本卦英文不把《易》的吉凶理解为宿命判决，也不把象辞改写成现代励志格
言； “吉、凶、悔、吝、厉、无咎”均按时位、德性、行动后果的关系处理。

第54 卦
䷵ 归妹 (Gui Mei)
The Marrying Maiden
原文
归妹，征凶，无攸利。
初九，归妹以娣，跛能履，征吉。
九二，眇能视，利幽人之贞。
六三，归妹以须，反归以娣。
九四，归妹愆期，迟归有时。
六五，帝乙归妹，其君之袂不如其娣之袂良。月几望，吉。
上六，女承筐无实，士刲羊无血，无攸利。
关键词释义
卦名 归妹（Gui Mei） ：婚姻失序之象；欲动而礼位不正。
英译标题 The Marrying Maiden。标题取意译，以便英语读者先得卦象主旨；拼音
保留专名身份。
归妹 少女归嫁；情欲先动而礼位失序。
征 出行、征伐或主动推进；须视卦爻时位判断可否。
吉 趋于善成的处境判断；不宜简化为 luck。
凶 趋于败坏或危害的处境判断；不作宿命论理解。
利 合宜而有益；不是 profit 或功利主义的私利。
贞 正固、守正、定向；英译多作 constancy。
时位 《易》以时与位判断行动是否相称；同一行为，得时得位则可吉，失时失位
则可凶。
189

190 第54 卦
中正 中谓不偏，正谓当位；二者是判断爻义的重要准则。
刚柔 阳刚与阴柔的动态配置；不是性别本质论，而是行为力量的结构。
贴近原文的英文直译
The Marrying Maiden: to campaign is misfortune; nothing is favorable.
Initial Nine: marrying the maiden as a younger sister; the lame can tread. Cam-
paigning good fortune.
Second Nine: the one-eyed can see; favorable for the secluded person’s constancy.
Third Six: marrying the maiden as a waiting maid; she returns and marries as
younger sister.
Fourth Nine: the marrying maiden misses the time; delayed marriage has its time.
Fifth Six: Di Yi gives his younger sister in marriage; the lady’s sleeves are not as
fine as her younger sister’s. The moon nearly full; good fortune.
Top Six: the woman carries a basket without contents; the man cuts a sheep without
blood. Nothing is favorable.
面向英语母语者的自然意译
In natural English, The Marrying Maiden may be read as a pattern of action rather
than a detached prediction. Its images show how timing, position, and moral mea-
sure govern success or danger.
The Marrying Maiden: to campaign is misfortune; nothing is favorable.
Initial Nine: marrying the maiden as a younger sister; the lame can tread. Cam-
paigning good fortune.
Second Nine: the one-eyed can see; favorable for the secluded person’s constancy.
Third Six: marrying the maiden as a waiting maid; she returns and marries as
younger sister.
Fourth Nine: the marrying maiden misses the time; delayed marriage has its time.
Fifth Six: Di Yi gives his younger sister in marriage; the lady’s sleeves are not as
fine as her younger sister’s. The moon nearly full; good fortune.
Top Six: the woman carries a basket without contents; the man cuts a sheep without
blood. Nothing is favorable.
最终推荐的深度文化译文
The Marrying Maiden: to campaign is misfortune; nothing is favorable.
Initial Nine: marrying the maiden as a younger sister; the lame can tread. Cam-
paigning good fortune.

one, the Great Person, constancy, trust, regret, misfortune, peril, and no blame, so
that an English reader can follow the ethical and symbolic grammar of the Changes
across all sixty-four hexagrams. It also avoids treating the text as either mechanical
divination or modern self-help prose; the judgment of each line depends on image,
timing, position, and conduct.
